Title: zMenu+ | GroupeZ Docs

URL Source: http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus

Published Time: Thu, 05 Mar 2026 10:45:40 GMT

Markdown Content:
*   [](https://docs.groupez.dev/)
*   zMenu+

zMenu+
------

**zMenu+** is the premium addon for zMenu that adds powerful advanced features to enhance your inventory creation experience.

What is zMenu+?[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus#what-is-zmenu "Direct link to What is zMenu+?")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

zMenu+ extends the capabilities of the free zMenu plugin with additional features designed for server owners who want even more control and functionality in their menus.

By purchasing zMenu+, you help keep zMenu **free for everyone**. Your support enables continued development and improvements to the free version that thousands of servers rely on.

Features[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus#features "Direct link to Features")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

zMenu+ includes exclusive features that are not available in the free version:

### Advanced Button Types[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus#advanced-button-types "Direct link to Advanced Button Types")

Additional button types for more complex menu behaviors.

### Enhanced Actions[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus#enhanced-actions "Direct link to Enhanced Actions")

Extra action types for more interactive menus.

### Premium Support[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus#premium-support "Direct link to Premium Support")

Priority support for zMenu+ customers.

### Early Access[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus#early-access "Direct link to Early Access")

Get access to new features before they're released in the free version.

Purchase[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus#purchase "Direct link to Purchase")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can purchase zMenu+ from:

*   **Minecraft Inventory Builder**: [https://minecraft-inventory-builder.com/resources/zmenu-addon](https://minecraft-inventory-builder.com/resources/zmenu-addon)
*   **SpigotMC**: [https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/zmenu-premium-zmenu-addon.115533/](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/zmenu-premium-zmenu-addon.115533/)

Installation[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus#installation "Direct link to Installation")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.   Purchase and download zMenu+ from the link above
2.   Make sure zMenu is already installed on your server
3.   Place the zMenu+ JAR file in your `plugins/` folder
4.   Restart your server

zMenu+ is an addon and requires the base zMenu plugin to function. Make sure you have zMenu installed first.

Support[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus#support "Direct link to Support")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For support with zMenu+:

*   **Discord**: [https://discord.groupez.dev](https://discord.groupez.dev/)
*   Create a ticket in the Discord server for priority support

Why Get zMenu+?[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus#why-get-zmenu "Direct link to Why Get zMenu+?")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you're using zMenu for a professional server and need:

*   More advanced features
*   Priority support
*   Early access to new features
*   Support the continued development of zMenu

Then zMenu+ is for you!

Free vs zMenu+ Comparison[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus#free-vs-zmenu-comparison "Direct link to Free vs zMenu+ Comparison")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Feature | zMenu (Free) | zMenu+ |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Basic Button Types | Yes | Yes |
| Advanced Button Types | Limited | All |
| Actions | 28+ types | Extended |
| Pattern System | Yes | Yes |
| Database Support | Yes | Yes |
| Support | Community | Priority |
| Updates | Regular | Early Access |
| Price | Free | Paid |

Frequently Asked Questions[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus#frequently-asked-questions "Direct link to Frequently Asked Questions")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Is zMenu+ required to use zMenu?[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus#is-zmenu-required-to-use-zmenu "Direct link to Is zMenu+ required to use zMenu?")

No, zMenu is fully functional as a free plugin. zMenu+ is optional and adds extra features.

### Can I try zMenu+ before buying?[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus#can-i-try-zmenu-before-buying "Direct link to Can I try zMenu+ before buying?")

Join the Discord server to see examples and ask questions about what zMenu+ offers.

### Is there a refund policy?[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus#is-there-a-refund-policy "Direct link to Is there a refund policy?")

Please check the Minecraft Inventory Builder website for their refund policy.

### Will my inventories work with zMenu+?[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus#will-my-inventories-work-with-zmenu "Direct link to Will my inventories work with zMenu+?")

Yes! zMenu+ is fully compatible with your existing zMenu configurations. It only adds new features - it doesn't change how existing features work.

================================================================================
Title: Commands & Permissions | GroupeZ Docs

URL Source: http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions

Published Time: Thu, 05 Mar 2026 10:45:39 GMT

Markdown Content:
This page lists all available commands and permissions in zMenu.

Main Command[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#main-command "Direct link to Main Command")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The main command is `/zm` (alias: `/zmenu`).

**Base Permission**: `zmenu.use`

Command List[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#command-list "Direct link to Command List")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### General Commands[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#general-commands "Direct link to General Commands")

| Command | Permission | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `/zm` | `zmenu.use` | Display the help menu |
| `/zm version` | - | Display plugin version information |
| `/zm list` | `zmenu.use` | List all loaded inventories |
| `/zm documentation` | `zmenu.documentation` | View documentation links |
| `/zm addons` | `zmenu.use` | List official addons |
| `/zm contributors` | `zmenu.use` | Show plugin contributors |

### Inventory Commands[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#inventory-commands "Direct link to Inventory Commands")

| Command | Permission | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `/zm open <inventory>` | `zmenu.open` | Open an inventory for yourself |
| `/zm open <inventory> <player>` | `zmenu.open` | Open an inventory for another player |
| `/zm open <inventory> <player> <args...>` | `zmenu.open` | Open inventory with arguments |
| `/zm create [name]` | `zmenu.create` | Create a new inventory from template |
| `/zm editor [name]` | `zmenu.editor` | Open the inventory editor |

**Examples:**

`/zm open shop/zm open shop Notch/zm open shop Notch "Welcome to the shop!"`

### Reload Commands[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#reload-commands "Direct link to Reload Commands")

| Command | Permission | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `/zm reload` | `zmenu.reload` | Reload all configurations |
| `/zm reload config` | `zmenu.reload` | Reload config.yml and messages only |
| `/zm reload inventory` | `zmenu.reload` | Reload all inventories |
| `/zm reload inventory <name>` | `zmenu.reload` | Reload a specific inventory |
| `/zm reload command` | `zmenu.reload` | Reload all commands |
| `/zm reload command <name>` | `zmenu.reload` | Reload a specific command |

**Examples:**

`/zm reload/zm reload inventory shop/zm reload command warp`

### Item Commands[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#item-commands "Direct link to Item Commands")

| Command | Permission | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `/zm giveitem <inventory> <player>` | `zmenu.giveitem` | Give a clickable item to player |
| `/zm giveopenitem <inventory> <player>` | `zmenu.giveopenitem` | Give menu-opening item to player |
| `/zm save <name>` | `zmenu.save` | Save held item as inventory |

### Player Data Commands[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#player-data-commands "Direct link to Player Data Commands")

| Command | Permission | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `/zm players add <player> <key> <value>` | `zmenu.players` | Add value to player data |
| `/zm players set <player> <key> <value>` | `zmenu.players` | Set player data value |
| `/zm players get <player> <key>` | `zmenu.players` | Get player data value |
| `/zm players remove <player> <key>` | `zmenu.players` | Remove player data key |
| `/zm players removeall <key>` | `zmenu.players` | Remove key from all players |
| `/zm players keys <player>` | `zmenu.players` | List all keys for a player |
| `/zm players convert` | `zmenu.players` | Convert JSON data to SQL |

**Examples:**

`/zm players set Notch coins 100/zm players add Notch coins 50/zm players get Notch coins/zm players keys Notch`

### Dialog Commands[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#dialog-commands "Direct link to Dialog Commands")

| Command | Permission | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `/zm dialog open <dialog>` | `zmenu.dialog` | Open a dialog for yourself |
| `/zm dialog open <dialog> <player>` | `zmenu.dialog` | Open a dialog for a player |

### Utility Commands[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#utility-commands "Direct link to Utility Commands")

| Command | Permission | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `/zm convert` | `zmenu.convert` | Convert configurations from other plugins |
| `/zm testdupe` | `zmenu.dupe` | Test the anti-dupe system |
| `/zm dumplog` | `zmenu.dumplog` | Export debug logs |

Permission List[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#permission-list "Direct link to Permission List")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Core Permissions[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#core-permissions "Direct link to Core Permissions")

| Permission | Description | Default |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `zmenu.use` | Access to basic commands | true |
| `zmenu.open` | Open inventories | op |
| `zmenu.open.bypass` | Bypass inventory open requirements | op |
| `zmenu.reload` | Reload configurations | op |
| `zmenu.create` | Create new inventories | op |
| `zmenu.editor` | Access inventory editor | op |

### Item Permissions[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#item-permissions "Direct link to Item Permissions")

| Permission | Description | Default |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `zmenu.giveitem` | Give clickable items | op |
| `zmenu.giveopenitem` | Give menu-opening items | op |
| `zmenu.save` | Save items as inventories | op |

### Player Data Permissions[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#player-data-permissions "Direct link to Player Data Permissions")

| Permission | Description | Default |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `zmenu.players` | Manage player data | op |

### Utility Permissions[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#utility-permissions "Direct link to Utility Permissions")

| Permission | Description | Default |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `zmenu.convert` | Convert from other plugins | op |
| `zmenu.dupe` | Test anti-dupe system | op |
| `zmenu.documentation` | View documentation | op |
| `zmenu.dialog` | Open dialogs | op |
| `zmenu.dumplog` | Export debug logs | op |

Custom Command Permissions[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#custom-command-permissions "Direct link to Custom Command Permissions")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you create custom commands in `commands/commands.yml`, you can define custom permissions:

`commands:  shop:    command: /shop    inventory: shop_menu    permission: myserver.shop    aliases:      - store      - market`

Players will need the `myserver.shop` permission to use `/shop`.

Inventory-Specific Permissions[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#inventory-specific-permissions "Direct link to Inventory-Specific Permissions")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can require specific permissions to open inventories using view requirements:

`# In your inventory fileview-requirement:  requirements:    - type: permission      permission: "myserver.vip.menu"      deny:        - type: message          messages:            - "&cYou need VIP to access this menu!"`

Admin Permission[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#admin-permission "Direct link to Admin Permission")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For server administrators, you can grant all zMenu permissions with:

`zmenu.*`

This grants access to all zMenu commands.

LuckPerms Examples[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#luckperms-examples "Direct link to LuckPerms Examples")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Grant basic usage:

`/lp user <player> permission set zmenu.use true`

Grant all admin permissions:

`/lp group admin permission set zmenu.* true`

Grant specific inventory access:

`/lp group vip permission set myserver.vip.menu true`

Permission Plugins[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#permission-plugins "Direct link to Permission Plugins")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

zMenu works with any permission plugin that supports Bukkit permissions:

*   LuckPerms (Recommended)
*   PermissionsEx
*   GroupManager
*   UltraPermissions
*   And many more

Next Steps[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/commands-permissions#next-steps "Direct link to Next Steps")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Learn about [Placeholders](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders)
*   Create [Custom Commands](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands)
*   Set up [Player Data](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/player-data) for persistent storage

Title: Placeholders | GroupeZ Docs

URL Source: http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders

Published Time: Thu, 05 Mar 2026 10:45:38 GMT

Markdown Content:
*   [](https://docs.groupez.dev/)
*   Configurations
*   Placeholders

Placeholders
------------

zMenu provides built-in placeholders and supports PlaceholderAPI for dynamic content in your inventories.

Built-in Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#built-in-placeholders "Direct link to Built-in Placeholders")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These placeholders are available without any additional plugins:

### Player Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#player-placeholders "Direct link to Player Placeholders")

| Placeholder | Description | Example Output |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `%player%` | Player's name | `Notch` |

### Pagination Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#pagination-placeholders "Direct link to Pagination Placeholders")

| Placeholder | Description | Example Output |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `%page%` | Current page number | `1` |
| `%maxPage%` | Maximum page number | `5` |
| `%max-page%` | Maximum page number (alias) | `5` |
| `%zmenu_player_page%` | Current page (PAPI format) | `1` |
| `%zmenu_player_next_page%` | Next page number | `2` |
| `%zmenu_player_previous_page%` | Previous page number | `0` |
| `%zmenu_player_max_page%` | Maximum page (PAPI format) | `5` |

### Inventory History Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#inventory-history-placeholders "Direct link to Inventory History Placeholders")

| Placeholder | Description | Example Output |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `%zmenu_player_previous_inventories%` | Number of previous inventories in history | `3` |

### Math Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#math-placeholders "Direct link to Math Placeholders")

Perform calculations directly in your configuration:

| Placeholder | Description | Example |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `%zmenu_math_<expression>%` | Calculate a math expression | `%zmenu_math_5+5%` → `10` |
| `%zmenu_formatted_math_<expression>%` | Formatted math result | `%zmenu_formatted_math_1000+500%` → `1,500` |

**Supported Operations:**

*   Addition: `+`
*   Subtraction: `-`
*   Multiplication: `*`
*   Division: `/`
*   Parentheses: `()`

**Examples:**

`lore:  - "&7Result: %zmenu_math_10*5%"           # Output: 50  - "&7Balance: %zmenu_formatted_math_%vault_eco_balance%*2%"`

### Player Data Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#player-data-placeholders "Direct link to Player Data Placeholders")

| Placeholder | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `%zmenu_player_value_<key>%` | Get player data value |

**Example:**

`lore:  - "&7Coins: &6%zmenu_player_value_coins%"  - "&7Kills: &c%zmenu_player_value_kills%"`

### Command Argument Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#command-argument-placeholders "Direct link to Command Argument Placeholders")

| Placeholder | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `%zmenu_argument_<key>%` | Get command argument value |

This placeholder retrieves arguments passed through custom commands configured in zMenu.

**Example:**

Command configuration:

`# In commands/commands.ymlcommands:  punish:    command: punish    arguments:      - player    inventory: example_punish`

Using the argument in your inventory:

`items:  player-info:    item:      material: PLAYER_HEAD      playerHead: "%zmenu_argument_player%"      name: "&cPunish %zmenu_argument_player%"      lore:        - "&7Click to punish this player"`

When a player runs `/punish Notch`, the placeholder `%zmenu_argument_player%` will return `Notch`.

### Global Placeholder Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#global-placeholder-placeholders "Direct link to Global Placeholder Placeholders")

| Placeholder | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `%zmenu_global_placeholders_<key>%` | Get global placeholder value |

**Example:**

`# In global-placeholders.ymlserver-name: "My Server"# In inventoryname: "&6%zmenu_global_placeholders_server-name%"`

### Time Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#time-placeholders "Direct link to Time Placeholders")

| Placeholder | Description | Example Output |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `%zmenu_time_unix_timestamp%` | Current Unix timestamp | `1704067200` |
| `%zmenu_time_next_day_unix_timestamp%` | Tomorrow's Unix timestamp | `1704153600` |
| `%zmenu_time_today_start_unix_timestamp%` | Start of today timestamp | `1704067200` |

### Statistic Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#statistic-placeholders "Direct link to Statistic Placeholders")

| Placeholder | Description | Example Output |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `%zmenu_statistic_hours_played%` | Hours played (rounded) | `42` |
| `%zmenu_statistic_time_played%` | Formatted playtime | `1d 18h 30m` |

PlaceholderAPI Integration[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#placeholderapi-integration "Direct link to PlaceholderAPI Integration")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

zMenu fully supports PlaceholderAPI. Any PAPI placeholder works in:

*   Inventory titles
*   Item names
*   Item lore
*   Messages
*   Requirements
*   Actions

### Popular PlaceholderAPI Expansions[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#popular-placeholderapi-expansions "Direct link to Popular PlaceholderAPI Expansions")

Install expansions with: `/papi ecloud download <name>`

| Expansion | Placeholders | Example |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Player | `%player_name%`, `%player_health%`, `%player_level%` | `%player_name%` → `Notch` |
| Vault | `%vault_eco_balance%`, `%vault_eco_balance_formatted%` | `%vault_eco_balance%` → `1500.00` |
| Statistic | `%statistic_deaths%`, `%statistic_kills%` | `%statistic_deaths%` → `42` |
| Server | `%server_online%`, `%server_max_players%` | `%server_online%` → `50` |
| LuckPerms | `%luckperms_prefix%`, `%luckperms_primary_group_name%` | `%luckperms_prefix%` → `[Admin]` |

### Using PlaceholderAPI[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#using-placeholderapi "Direct link to Using PlaceholderAPI")

`items:  profile:    slot: 4    item:      material: PLAYER_HEAD      playerHead: "%player_name%"      name: "&6%player_name%'s Profile"      lore:        - "&8&m─────────────────"        - ""        - "&7Health: &c%player_health%&7/&c%player_max_health%"        - "&7Level: &a%player_level%"        - "&7Balance: &6$%vault_eco_balance_formatted%"        - ""        - "&7Kills: &a%statistic_player_kills%"        - "&7Deaths: &c%statistic_deaths%"        - ""        - "&8&m─────────────────"`

Local Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#local-placeholders "Direct link to Local Placeholders")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Define placeholders specific to an inventory:

`# In your inventory filelocal-placeholders:  price: "100"  item-name: "Special Sword"items:  shop-item:    item:      name: "&6%item-name%"      lore:        - "&7Price: &a$%price%"`

Placeholder Caching[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#placeholder-caching "Direct link to Placeholder Caching")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For better performance, you can enable placeholder caching in `config.yml`:

`# Enable PlaceholderAPI cachingenable-cache-placeholder-api: true# Cache duration in ticks (20 ticks = 1 second)cache-placeholder-api: 20`

Caching means placeholders won't update instantly. Only enable this if you have performance issues and understand the implications.

Nested Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#nested-placeholders "Direct link to Nested Placeholders")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use placeholders inside other placeholders:

`# Using player data in mathlore:  - "&7Double coins: %zmenu_math_%zmenu_player_value_coins%*2%"`

Requirements with Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#requirements-with-placeholders "Direct link to Requirements with Placeholders")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use placeholders in requirements to create dynamic conditions:

`click-requirement:  requirements:    - type: placeholder      placeholder: "%vault_eco_balance%"      action: SUPERIOR_OR_EQUAL      value: 100      deny:        - type: message          messages:            - "&cYou need at least $100!"`

Placeholder Formatting[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#placeholder-formatting "Direct link to Placeholder Formatting")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Numbers[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#numbers "Direct link to Numbers")

For formatted numbers, use the `_formatted` variants when available:

*   `%vault_eco_balance_formatted%` instead of `%vault_eco_balance%`
*   `%zmenu_formatted_math_<expr>%` instead of `%zmenu_math_<expr>%`

### Colors in Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#colors-in-placeholders "Direct link to Colors in Placeholders")

Some placeholders include color codes. To strip them:

`name: "%luckperms_prefix% %player_name%"  # Keeps colors`

Debugging Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#debugging-placeholders "Direct link to Debugging Placeholders")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If placeholders aren't working:

1.   **Check PlaceholderAPI is installed**

`/papi info` 
2.   **Test the placeholder**

`/papi parse me %placeholder_name%` 
3.   **Check the expansion is installed**

`/papi list` 
4.   **Install missing expansions**

`/papi ecloud download <expansion>/papi reload` 

Quick Reference Table[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#quick-reference-table "Direct link to Quick Reference Table")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Category | Placeholder | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Player | `%player%` | Player name |
| Page | `%page%` | Current page |
| Page | `%maxPage%` | Max page |
| Math | `%zmenu_math_<expr>%` | Calculate expression |
| Data | `%zmenu_player_value_<key>%` | Player data |
| Argument | `%zmenu_argument_<key>%` | Command argument |
| Global | `%zmenu_global_placeholders_<key>%` | Global value |
| Time | `%zmenu_time_unix_timestamp%` | Unix time |
| Stats | `%zmenu_statistic_hours_played%` | Hours played |

Next Steps[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders#next-steps "Direct link to Next Steps")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Title: Inventory Configuration | GroupeZ Docs

URL Source: http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory

Published Time: Thu, 05 Mar 2026 10:45:39 GMT

Markdown Content:
*   [](https://docs.groupez.dev/)
*   Configurations
*   Inventories
*   Inventory Configuration

Inventory Configuration
-----------------------

This page documents all available configuration options for creating inventories in zMenu.

File Location[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#file-location "Direct link to File Location")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Inventories are stored in the `plugins/zMenu/inventories/` folder. Each YAML file represents one inventory. You can organize inventories in subfolders.

`plugins/zMenu/inventories/├── main_menu.yml├── shop.yml├── warps/│   ├── spawn.yml│   └── hub.yml└── admin/    └── admin_menu.yml`

Basic Structure[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#basic-structure "Direct link to Basic Structure")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`# Inventory name displayed in the title barname: "&6My Inventory"# Inventory size (9, 18, 27, 36, 45, or 54)size: 54# Enable or disable this inventoryenable: true# Button definitionsitems:  button-name:    # Button configuration...`

Configuration Options[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#configuration-options "Direct link to Configuration Options")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### name[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#name "Direct link to name")

The title displayed at the top of the inventory.

`name: "&6&lMy Server Menu"`

**Features:**

*   Supports color codes (`&6`, `&#FF5500`)
*   Supports MiniMessage (if enabled)
*   Supports placeholders (`%player%`, `%page%`)

**Pagination placeholders:**

`name: "&6Shop &7(Page %page%/%max-page%)"`

* * *

### size[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#size "Direct link to size")

The number of slots in the inventory. Must be a multiple of 9 (for CHEST type).

| Size | Rows | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 9 | 1 | Single row |
| 18 | 2 | Two rows |
| 27 | 3 | Three rows (small chest) |
| 36 | 4 | Four rows |
| 45 | 5 | Five rows |
| 54 | 6 | Six rows (double chest) |

`size: 54`

* * *

### type[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#type "Direct link to type")

The inventory type. Defines the visual layout of the inventory.

`type: CHEST`

**Available types:**

| Type | Size | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `CHEST` | 9-54 | Standard chest inventory (default) |
| `DISPENSER` | 9 | 3x3 dispenser layout |
| `DROPPER` | 9 | 3x3 dropper layout |
| `FURNACE` | 3 | Furnace layout |
| `WORKBENCH` | 10 | Crafting table layout |
| `ENCHANTING` | 2 | Enchanting table layout |
| `BREWING` | 5 | Brewing stand layout |
| `ANVIL` | 3 | Anvil layout |
| `BEACON` | 1 | Beacon layout |
| `HOPPER` | 5 | Hopper layout (5 slots) |
| `SHULKER_BOX` | 27 | Shulker box layout |
| `BARREL` | 27 | Barrel layout |
| `BLAST_FURNACE` | 3 | Blast furnace layout |
| `LECTERN` | 1 | Lectern layout |
| `SMOKER` | 3 | Smoker layout |
| `LOOM` | 4 | Loom layout |
| `CARTOGRAPHY` | 3 | Cartography table layout |
| `GRINDSTONE` | 3 | Grindstone layout |
| `STONECUTTER` | 2 | Stonecutter layout |
| `SMITHING` | 4 | Smithing table layout |

When using a type other than `CHEST`, the `size` option is ignored as each type has a fixed size.

**Example with hopper:**

`name: "&8Quick Select"type: HOPPERitems:  option1:    slot: 0    item:      material: DIAMOND      name: "&bOption 1"`

* * *

### enable[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#enable "Direct link to enable")

Enable or disable this inventory. Disabled inventories cannot be opened.

`enable: true`

This is useful for temporarily disabling an inventory without deleting the file.

* * *

### update-interval[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#update-interval "Direct link to update-interval")

Automatically refresh the inventory at a regular interval (in milliseconds).

`update-interval: 1000  # Refresh every second (1000ms)`

1000ms = 1 second. Use this for inventories with dynamic placeholders that need frequent updates.

* * *

### title-animation[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#title-animation "Direct link to title-animation")

Animate the inventory title with multiple frames. This creates a dynamic title that cycles through different text values.

This feature **requires**[PacketEvents](https://github.com/retrooper/packetevents) to be installed on your server. Without PacketEvents, title animations will not work.

`title-animation:  titles:    - "&bWelcome to &aMenu!"    - "&eEnjoy &four &9Features!"    - "&cRotating &6Animated &2Title!"  cycles: 5  initial-delay: 1  interval: 2  time-unit: SECONDS  show-items-after-animation: true  item-update-interval: 1`

**Configuration options:**

| Option | Type | Default | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `titles` | List | - | List of title frames to cycle through |
| `cycles` | Integer | -1 | Number of animation cycles (-1 for infinite) |
| `initial-delay` | Integer | 0 | Delay before animation starts |
| `interval` | Integer | 1 | Time between each frame |
| `time-unit` | String | SECONDS | Time unit for delays (SECONDS, MILLISECONDS, TICKS) |
| `show-items-after-animation` | Boolean | true | Show items after animation completes |
| `item-update-interval` | Integer | 1 | How often to update items during animation |

**Time units:**

*   `NANOSECONDS`
*   `MICROSECONDS`
*   `MILLISECONDS`
*   `SECONDS`
*   `MINUTES`
*   `HOURS`
*   `DAYS`

**Complete example:**

`name: "&6Loading..."size: 27title-animation:  titles:    - "&6&l⏳ Loading."    - "&6&l⏳ Loading.."    - "&6&l⏳ Loading..."    - "&a&l✓ Welcome!"  cycles: 1  initial-delay: 0  interval: 500  time-unit: MILLISECONDS  show-items-after-animation: trueitems:  content:    slot: 13    item:      material: NETHER_STAR      name: "&eMenu Content"`

* * *

### clear-inventory[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#clear-inventory "Direct link to clear-inventory")

Clear the player's inventory while the menu is open and restore it when closed.

`clear-inventory: true`

**Use cases:**

*   Custom texture packs that overlay the entire screen
*   Preventing item interaction while in menu

* * *

### cancel-item-pickup[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#cancel-item-pickup "Direct link to cancel-item-pickup")

Prevent players from picking up items while the inventory is open.

`cancel-item-pickup: true`

**Use cases:**

*   Preventing accidental item pickup during menu interaction
*   Clean GUI experience without interference

* * *

### target-player-name-placeholder[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#target-player-name-placeholder "Direct link to target-player-name-placeholder")

Define a custom placeholder for the target player's name. Useful when opening inventories for other players.

`target-player-name-placeholder: "%target%"`

**Default:**`%player_name%`

**Example usage:**

`name: "&6Profile of %target%"target-player-name-placeholder: "%target%"items:  info:    slot: 13    item:      material: PLAYER_HEAD      name: "&e%target%"      lore:        - "&7Viewing player profile"`

* * *

### action-patterns[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#action-patterns "Direct link to action-patterns")

Apply action patterns to all buttons in this inventory. Action patterns are reusable sets of actions defined in the `plugins/zMenu/action_patterns/` folder.

`action-patterns:  - "default-actions"  - "click-sound"`

**Action pattern file example** (`plugins/zMenu/action_patterns/default-actions.yml`):

`name: default-actionsactions:  - type: sound    sound: ENTITY_VILLAGER_YESdeny-actions:  - type: sound    sound: ENTITY_VILLAGER_NO`

When applied, all buttons in the inventory will inherit these actions. Button-specific actions are executed after pattern actions.

* * *

### fill-item[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#fill-item "Direct link to fill-item")

Define an item to fill all empty slots.

`fill-item:  material: BLACK_STAINED_GLASS_PANE  name: "&8"`

This automatically fills any slot not occupied by a button.

* * *

### patterns[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#patterns "Direct link to patterns")

Apply reusable patterns to this inventory.

`patterns:  - "navigation_bar"  - "border_pattern"`

Patterns must be defined in the `plugins/zMenu/patterns/` folder. See [Patterns](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/patterns) for details.

* * *

### matrix[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#matrix "Direct link to matrix")

Define the inventory layout visually using characters.

`matrix:  - "AAAAAAAAA"  - "A       A"  - "A   B   A"  - "A       A"  - "AAAAAAAAA"items:  A:    item:      material: BLACK_STAINED_GLASS_PANE      name: "&8"  B:    item:      material: DIAMOND      name: "&bCenter Item"`

Each character represents an item. Spaces are empty slots.

* * *

### items[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#items "Direct link to items")

The buttons in your inventory. This is where you define all clickable elements.

`items:  my-button:    slot: 0    item:      material: DIAMOND      name: "&bDiamond"    actions:      - type: message        messages:          - "&aYou clicked the diamond!"  another-button:    slot: 8    item:      material: EMERALD      name: "&aEmerald"`

See [Button Configuration](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/button) for complete button documentation.

* * *

### view-requirement[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#view-requirement "Direct link to view-requirement")

Requirements that must be met to open this inventory.

`view-requirement:  requirements:    - type: permission      permission: "myserver.vip"      deny:        - type: message          messages:            - "&cYou need VIP to access this menu!"`

If requirements aren't met, the inventory won't open and deny actions will execute.

* * *

### open-requirement[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#open-requirement "Direct link to open-requirement")

Alternative name for view-requirement (same functionality).

`open-requirement:  requirements:    - type: permission      permission: "myserver.premium"`

* * *

### open-with-item[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#open-with-item "Direct link to open-with-item")

Define an item that opens this inventory when held and clicked.

`open-with-item:  item:    material: COMPASS    name: "&6&lMenu"    lore:      - "&7Right-click to open"  actions:    - RIGHT_CLICK    - RIGHT_CLICK_BLOCK  type: full  # full, contains, or starts_with`

**Actions types:**

*   `RIGHT_CLICK` - Right click in air
*   `LEFT_CLICK` - Left click in air
*   `RIGHT_CLICK_BLOCK` - Right click on a block
*   `LEFT_CLICK_BLOCK` - Left click on a block

**Type options:**

*   `full` - Item must match exactly
*   `contains` - Item name must contain the specified name
*   `starts_with` - Item name must start with the specified name

Give players the item with:

`/zm giveopenitem <inventory> <player>`

* * *

### open-actions[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#open-actions "Direct link to open-actions")

Actions to execute when the inventory opens.

`open-actions:  - type: sound    sound: ENTITY_EXPERIENCE_ORB_PICKUP  - type: message    messages:      - "&aWelcome to the menu!"`

* * *

### close-actions[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#close-actions "Direct link to close-actions")

Actions to execute when the inventory closes.

`close-actions:  - type: message    messages:      - "&7Thanks for visiting!"`

* * *

### local-placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#local-placeholders "Direct link to local-placeholders")

Define inventory-specific placeholders.

`local-placeholders:  server-ip: "play.myserver.com"  discord: "discord.gg/myserver"items:  info:    item:      lore:        - "&7IP: &f%server-ip%"        - "&7Discord: &f%discord%"`

* * *

Complete Example[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#complete-example "Direct link to Complete Example")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`name: "&6&lServer Menu &7(&f%page%&7/&f%maxPage%&7)"size: 54enable: trueupdate-interval: 2000  # 2 secondsfill-item:  material: GRAY_STAINED_GLASS_PANE  name: "&8"patterns:  - "navigation"view-requirement:  requirements:    - type: permission      permission: "server.menu.use"      deny:        - type: message          messages:            - "&cYou don't have permission to use this menu!"open-actions:  - type: sound    sound: BLOCK_CHEST_OPEN    pitch: 1.2close-actions:  - type: sound    sound: BLOCK_CHEST_CLOSElocal-placeholders:  menu-version: "1.0"items:  title:    slot: 4    item:      material: NETHER_STAR      name: "&6&lServer Menu"      lore:        - "&8Version %menu-version%"        - ""        - "&7Welcome, &f%player%&7!"        - ""        - "&7Select an option below."  teleports:    slot: 20    item:      material: ENDER_PEARL      name: "&b&lTeleports"      lore:        - "&7Access teleportation options"    actions:      - type: inventory        inventory: "teleports_menu"  shop:    slot: 22    item:      material: GOLD_INGOT      name: "&e&lShop"      lore:        - "&7Buy and sell items"    actions:      - type: inventory        inventory: "shop_menu"  settings:    slot: 24    item:      material: COMPARATOR      name: "&c&lSettings"      lore:        - "&7Configure your preferences"    actions:      - type: inventory        inventory: "settings_menu"  close:    slot: 49    item:      material: BARRIER      name: "&c&lClose"      lore:        - "&7Close this menu"    actions:      - type: close`

Multi-Page Inventories[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#multi-page-inventories "Direct link to Multi-Page Inventories")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

zMenu automatically creates pagination when buttons have multiple slots or pages defined:

`items:  shop-item:    slots:      - 10-16      - 19-25      - 28-34    item:      # This will create multiple pages if there are more items than slots`

Use `NEXT` and `PREVIOUS` button types for navigation. See [Button Types](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/next) for details.

Best Practices[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#best-practices "Direct link to Best Practices")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.   **Organize your inventories** in subfolders by category
2.   **Use patterns** for repeated elements like borders
3.   **Use local placeholders** for values used multiple times
4.   **Test with `/zm reload inventory <name>`** for quick iteration
5.   **Use meaningful button names** for easier maintenance
6.   **Keep inventory sizes appropriate** - don't use 54 slots if you only need 27

Next Steps[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/inventories/inventory#next-steps "Direct link to Next Steps")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Config.yml
----------

The `config.yml` file is the main configuration file for zMenu. It controls global plugin settings, database configuration, performance options, and more.

File Location[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#file-location "Direct link to File Location")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`plugins/zMenu/config.yml`

Complete Configuration Reference[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#complete-configuration-reference "Direct link to Complete Configuration Reference")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`########################################          Debug Settings             ######################################### Enable debug messages in consoleenable-debug: false# Enable debug timing informationenable-debug-time: false########################################         Storage Settings            ######################################### Storage type for player data# Options: SQLITE, MYSQL, MARIADB, NONEstorage-type: SQLITE# Database configuration (for MySQL/MariaDB)database-configuration:  table-prefix: "zmenu_"  host: "localhost"  port: 3306  user: "username"  password: "password"  database: "zmenu"########################################        Formatting Settings          ######################################### Enable MiniMessage format (Paper/Purpur only)# This allows modern formatting like <gradient:red:blue>enable-mini-message-format: true########################################        Performance Settings         ######################################### Cache item stacks for better performanceenable-cache-item-stack: true# Enable PlaceholderAPI cachingenable-cache-placeholder-api: false# PlaceholderAPI cache duration (ticks, 20 = 1 second)cache-placeholder-api: 20# Cache offline player data (seconds)cache-offline-player: 300########################################           Click Settings            ######################################### Enable click cooldown to prevent spam clickingenable-cooldown-click: true# Cooldown duration (milliseconds)cooldown-click-milliseconds: 100########################################         Security Settings           ######################################### Enable anti-dupe protectionenable-anti-dupe: true# Log when players open inventoriesenable-player-open-inventory-logs: true########################################          Menu Settings              ######################################### Default main menu inventory namemain-menu: "example"# Use swap item offhand key (F) to open main menuuse-swap-item-off-hand-key-to-open-main-menu: false`

Configuration Options Explained[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#configuration-options-explained "Direct link to Configuration Options Explained")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Debug Settings[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#debug-settings "Direct link to Debug Settings")

#### enable-debug[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#enable-debug "Direct link to enable-debug")

Enables detailed debug messages in the console. Useful for troubleshooting issues.

`enable-debug: false`

**When to enable:**

*   Troubleshooting inventory loading issues
*   Debugging placeholder problems
*   Reporting bugs to the developer

* * *

#### enable-debug-time[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#enable-debug-time "Direct link to enable-debug-time")

Shows timing information for operations.

`enable-debug-time: false`

* * *

### Storage Settings[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#storage-settings "Direct link to Storage Settings")

#### storage-type[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#storage-type "Direct link to storage-type")

Determines how player data is stored.

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `SQLITE` | Local file-based database (default) |
| `MYSQL` | MySQL server |
| `MARIADB` | MariaDB server |
| `NONE` | No persistent storage |

`storage-type: SQLITE`

**Recommendations:**

*   **Single server**: Use `SQLITE`
*   **Network/BungeeCord**: Use `MYSQL` or `MARIADB`
*   **No player data needed**: Use `NONE`

* * *

#### database-configuration[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#database-configuration "Direct link to database-configuration")

MySQL/MariaDB connection settings.

`database-configuration:  table-prefix: "zmenu_"  host: "localhost"  port: 3306  user: "minecraft"  password: "secure_password"  database: "minecraft_db"`

| Option | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `table-prefix` | Prefix for database tables |
| `host` | Database server address |
| `port` | Database port (default: 3306) |
| `user` | Database username |
| `password` | Database password |
| `database` | Database name |

* * *

### Formatting Settings[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#formatting-settings "Direct link to Formatting Settings")

#### enable-mini-message-format[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#enable-mini-message-format "Direct link to enable-mini-message-format")

Enables MiniMessage formatting for text. **Only works on Paper/Purpur/Pufferfish**.

`enable-mini-message-format: true`

When enabled, you can use:

`name: "<gradient:red:blue>Gradient Text</gradient>"lore:  - "<rainbow>Rainbow!</rainbow>"  - "<bold><gold>Bold gold</gold></bold>"`

* * *

### Performance Settings[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#performance-settings "Direct link to Performance Settings")

#### enable-cache-item-stack[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#enable-cache-item-stack "Direct link to enable-cache-item-stack")

Caches created ItemStacks to improve performance.

`enable-cache-item-stack: true`

**Recommendation:** Keep enabled unless you experience issues.

* * *

#### enable-cache-placeholder-api[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#enable-cache-placeholder-api "Direct link to enable-cache-placeholder-api")

Caches PlaceholderAPI results to reduce parsing overhead.

`enable-cache-placeholder-api: false`

Enabling this means placeholders won't update instantly. Use with caution.

* * *

#### cache-placeholder-api[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#cache-placeholder-api "Direct link to cache-placeholder-api")

Duration to cache placeholder results (in ticks).

`cache-placeholder-api: 20  # 1 second`

* * *

#### cache-offline-player[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#cache-offline-player "Direct link to cache-offline-player")

How long to cache offline player data (seconds).

`cache-offline-player: 300  # 5 minutes`

* * *

### Click Settings[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#click-settings "Direct link to Click Settings")

#### enable-cooldown-click[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#enable-cooldown-click "Direct link to enable-cooldown-click")

Prevents spam clicking by adding a cooldown between clicks.

`enable-cooldown-click: true`

* * *

#### cooldown-click-milliseconds[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#cooldown-click-milliseconds "Direct link to cooldown-click-milliseconds")

The cooldown duration between clicks.

`cooldown-click-milliseconds: 100  # 0.1 seconds`

**Adjust based on your needs:**

*   Lower = More responsive, risk of accidental double-clicks
*   Higher = Safer, might feel sluggish

* * *

### Security Settings[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#security-settings "Direct link to Security Settings")

#### enable-anti-dupe[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#enable-anti-dupe "Direct link to enable-anti-dupe")

Enables the anti-item-duplication system.

`enable-anti-dupe: true`

This detects and prevents common item duplication exploits involving inventory GUIs.

* * *

#### enable-player-open-inventory-logs[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#enable-player-open-inventory-logs "Direct link to enable-player-open-inventory-logs")

Logs when players open zMenu inventories.

`enable-player-open-inventory-logs: true`

Useful for:

*   Monitoring player activity
*   Debugging issues
*   Security auditing

* * *

### Menu Settings[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#menu-settings "Direct link to Menu Settings")

#### main-menu[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#main-menu "Direct link to main-menu")

The default inventory opened by the `MAIN_MENU` button type and the F key shortcut.

`main-menu: "example"`

This should match an inventory filename (without `.yml`) in your `inventories/` folder.

* * *

#### use-swap-item-off-hand-key-to-open-main-menu[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#use-swap-item-off-hand-key-to-open-main-menu "Direct link to use-swap-item-off-hand-key-to-open-main-menu")

Allow players to press F (swap offhand key) to open the main menu.

`use-swap-item-off-hand-key-to-open-main-menu: false`

**When to enable:**

*   You want easy menu access without commands
*   Your server has a main hub menu

**When to keep disabled:**

*   Players need the F key for actual item swapping
*   You use custom resource packs with F key bindings

* * *

Example Configurations[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#example-configurations "Direct link to Example Configurations")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Basic Server (SQLite)[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#basic-server-sqlite "Direct link to Basic Server (SQLite)")

`enable-debug: falsestorage-type: SQLITEenable-mini-message-format: trueenable-cache-item-stack: trueenable-anti-dupe: trueenable-cooldown-click: truecooldown-click-milliseconds: 100main-menu: "main"`

### Network Server (MySQL)[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#network-server-mysql "Direct link to Network Server (MySQL)")

`enable-debug: falsestorage-type: MYSQLdatabase-configuration:  table-prefix: "zmenu_"  host: "mysql.mynetwork.com"  port: 3306  user: "zmenu_user"  password: "secure_password_here"  database: "minecraft_network"enable-mini-message-format: trueenable-cache-item-stack: trueenable-cache-placeholder-api: truecache-placeholder-api: 40enable-anti-dupe: truemain-menu: "hub_menu"`

### Performance-Focused[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#performance-focused "Direct link to Performance-Focused")

`enable-debug: falsestorage-type: SQLITEenable-cache-item-stack: trueenable-cache-placeholder-api: truecache-placeholder-api: 60cache-offline-player: 600enable-cooldown-click: truecooldown-click-milliseconds: 150`

### Development/Testing[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#developmenttesting "Direct link to Development/Testing")

`enable-debug: trueenable-debug-time: truestorage-type: SQLITEenable-cache-item-stack: falseenable-cache-placeholder-api: falseenable-cooldown-click: falseenable-player-open-inventory-logs: true`

Reloading Configuration[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#reloading-configuration "Direct link to Reloading Configuration")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After making changes:

`/zm reload config`

Or reload everything:

`/zm reload`

Database configuration changes require a server restart to take effect.

Best Practices[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#best-practices "Direct link to Best Practices")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.   **Start with defaults**: Only change what you need
2.   **Enable caching on large servers**: Improves performance
3.   **Use MySQL for networks**: Allows data sharing across servers
4.   **Keep anti-dupe enabled**: Protects your economy
5.   **Test debug mode**: Useful when setting up, disable in production
6.   **Set appropriate click cooldown**: Balance responsiveness and safety

Troubleshooting[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#troubleshooting "Direct link to Troubleshooting")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Database Connection Failed[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#database-connection-failed "Direct link to Database Connection Failed")

1.   Verify credentials are correct
2.   Check database server is running
3.   Ensure the database exists
4.   Check firewall allows connections
5.   Verify user has proper permissions

### Placeholders Not Updating[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#placeholders-not-updating "Direct link to Placeholders Not Updating")

1.   Disable placeholder caching temporarily
2.   Check if PlaceholderAPI is installed
3.   Verify the expansion is downloaded

### Performance Issues[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml#performance-issues "Direct link to Performance Issues")

1.   Enable item stack caching
2.   Enable placeholder caching
3.   Increase click cooldown
4.   Check for inventory loops (A opens B opens A)

Title: Supported Plugins | GroupeZ Docs

URL Source: http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins

Published Time: Thu, 05 Mar 2026 10:45:40 GMT

Markdown Content:
*   [](https://docs.groupez.dev/)
*   Supported Plugins

Supported Plugins
-----------------

zMenu integrates with many popular Minecraft plugins to extend its functionality. This page lists all officially supported plugins and what features they enable.

Placeholder Plugins[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#placeholder-plugins "Direct link to Placeholder Plugins")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### PlaceholderAPI[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#placeholderapi "Direct link to PlaceholderAPI")

**Download**: [SpigotMC](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/placeholderapi.6245/)

PlaceholderAPI is highly recommended for zMenu. It allows you to display dynamic values in your inventories, such as player statistics, economy balances, and much more.

**Features enabled:**

*   Use `%placeholder%` syntax in item names, lore, and messages
*   Thousands of available expansions
*   Cached placeholder parsing for performance

**Example:**

`item:  material: DIAMOND  name: "&6%player_name%'s Menu"  lore:    - "&7Balance: &a$%vault_eco_balance%"    - "&7Playtime: &e%statistic_hours_played%h"`

* * *

Economy Plugins[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#economy-plugins "Direct link to Economy Plugins")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Vault[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#vault "Direct link to Vault")

**Download**: [SpigotMC](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/vault.34315/)

Vault provides a unified economy API that zMenu uses for currency-based actions.

**Features enabled:**

*   `currency-deposit` action
*   `currency-withdraw` action
*   Economy placeholders

* * *

Permission Plugins[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#permission-plugins "Direct link to Permission Plugins")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### LuckPerms[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#luckperms "Direct link to LuckPerms")

**Download**: [https://luckperms.net/](https://luckperms.net/)

LuckPerms integration allows for advanced permission-based features.

**Features enabled:**

*   `luckperm` requirement type
*   `luckperm-set` action to modify player groups
*   Group-based view requirements

**Example:**

`click-requirement:  requirements:    - type: luckperm      group: vip      deny:        - type: message          messages:            - "&cYou need VIP rank to use this!"`

* * *

Custom Item Plugins[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#custom-item-plugins "Direct link to Custom Item Plugins")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### ItemsAdder[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#itemsadder "Direct link to ItemsAdder")

**Download**: [SpigotMC](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/itemsadder.73355/)

ItemsAdder allows you to use custom items with textures in your menus.

**Usage:**

`item:  material: ITEMSADDER:namespace:item_id`

* * *

### Oraxen[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#oraxen "Direct link to Oraxen")

**Download**: [SpigotMC](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/oraxen.72448/)

Oraxen support for custom items and models.

**Usage:**

`item:  material: ORAXEN:item_id`

* * *

### HeadDatabase[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#headdatabase "Direct link to HeadDatabase")

**Download**: [SpigotMC](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/head-database.14280/)

HeadDatabase provides thousands of custom player head textures.

**Usage:**

`item:  material: HEAD_DATABASE:12345`

* * *

### Slimefun[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#slimefun "Direct link to Slimefun")

**Download**: [GitHub](https://github.com/Slimefun/Slimefun4)

Use Slimefun items in your menus.

**Usage:**

`item:  material: SLIMEFUN:ITEM_ID`

* * *

### MythicMobs[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#mythicmobs "Direct link to MythicMobs")

**Download**: [SpigotMC](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/mythicmobs.5702/)

MythicMobs integration for custom items.

**Usage:**

`item:  material: MYTHICMOBS:item_id`

* * *

### ExecutableItems[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#executableitems "Direct link to ExecutableItems")

**Download**: [SpigotMC](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/executableitems.77578/)

ExecutableItems support for special items.

**Usage:**

`item:  material: EXECUTABLE_ITEM:item_id`

* * *

### ExecutableBlocks[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#executableblocks "Direct link to ExecutableBlocks")

**Download**: [SpigotMC](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/executableblocks.96914/)

ExecutableBlocks support for special blocks as items.

* * *

### BreweryX[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#breweryx "Direct link to BreweryX")

**Download**: [SpigotMC](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/breweryx.114777/)

BreweryX integration for brewing system items.

**Usage:**

`item:  material: BREWERYX:recipe_name`

* * *

Head Plugins[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#head-plugins "Direct link to Head Plugins")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### zHead[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#zhead "Direct link to zHead")

**Download**: [SpigotMC](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/zhead.115717/)

Another head texture plugin by the same developer.

**Usage:**

`item:  material: ZHEAD:category:head_name`

* * *

### HMCCosmetics[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#hmccosmetics "Direct link to HMCCosmetics")

**Download**: [SpigotMC](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/hmccosmetics.100107/)

HMCCosmetics integration for cosmetic items.

* * *

### MagicCosmetics[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#magiccosmetics "Direct link to MagicCosmetics")

MagicCosmetics integration for cosmetic items.

* * *

Job Plugins[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#job-plugins "Direct link to Job Plugins")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Jobs Reborn[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#jobs-reborn "Direct link to Jobs Reborn")

**Download**: [SpigotMC](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/jobs-reborn.4216/)

Jobs Reborn integration for job-based requirements.

**Features enabled:**

*   `job` requirement type to check job levels

**Example:**

`click-requirement:  requirements:    - type: job      job: Miner      level: 10`

* * *

Shopkeeper Plugins[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#shopkeeper-plugins "Direct link to Shopkeeper Plugins")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Shopkeepers[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#shopkeepers "Direct link to Shopkeepers")

Integration with Shopkeepers plugin.

**Features enabled:**

*   `shopkeeper` action type

* * *

Packet Plugins[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#packet-plugins "Direct link to Packet Plugins")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### PacketEvents[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#packetevents "Direct link to PacketEvents")

**Download**: [SpigotMC](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/packetevents-api.80279/)

PacketEvents is required for the Dialog system (Minecraft 1.20.5+).

**Features enabled:**

*   Dialog system support
*   Advanced UI features

* * *

Supported Plugin Summary Table[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#supported-plugin-summary-table "Direct link to Supported Plugin Summary Table")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Plugin | Category | Material Prefix | Feature |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| PlaceholderAPI | Placeholders | - | Dynamic values |
| Vault | Economy | - | Currency actions |
| LuckPerms | Permissions | - | Group requirements |
| ItemsAdder | Custom Items | `ITEMSADDER:` | Custom items/textures |
| Oraxen | Custom Items | `ORAXEN:` | Custom items/models |
| HeadDatabase | Heads | `HEAD_DATABASE:` | Custom heads |
| Slimefun | Custom Items | `SLIMEFUN:` | Slimefun items |
| MythicMobs | Custom Items | `MYTHICMOBS:` | MythicMobs items |
| ExecutableItems | Custom Items | `EXECUTABLE_ITEM:` | EI items |
| BreweryX | Custom Items | `BREWERYX:` | Brewing items |
| zHead | Heads | `ZHEAD:` | Custom heads |
| Jobs Reborn | Jobs | - | Job requirements |
| PacketEvents | Packets | - | Dialog system |

Using Custom Materials[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#using-custom-materials "Direct link to Using Custom Materials")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When using custom item plugins, the material format typically follows this pattern:

`item:  material: PLUGIN_PREFIX:item_identifier`

### Examples:[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#examples "Direct link to Examples:")

`# ItemsAdderitem:  material: ITEMSADDER:my_namespace:ruby# Oraxenitem:  material: ORAXEN:emerald_sword# HeadDatabaseitem:  material: HEAD_DATABASE:1234# Slimefunitem:  material: SLIMEFUN:ELECTRIC_MOTOR# MythicMobsitem:  material: MYTHICMOBS:SkeletonKingSword`

Plugin Detection[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/supported-plugins#plugin-detection "Direct link to Plugin Detection")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

zMenu automatically detects installed plugins and enables their features. You don't need to configure anything - just install the plugins and restart your server.

To verify which plugins zMenu detected, check the console output when the server starts or use the `/zm version` command.

[](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/installation)[](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus)

Title: DYNAMIC_PAGINATION Button | GroupeZ Docs

URL Source: http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/dynamic-pagination

Markdown Content:
*   [](https://docs.groupez.dev/)
*   Configurations
*   Buttons
*   Button Types
*   DYNAMIC_PAGINATION Button

DYNAMIC_PAGINATION Button Type
------------------------------

This button type requires [zMenu+](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus) to work.

The `DYNAMIC_PAGINATION` button type allows you to display dynamically generated paginated content. Unlike regular `PAGINATION`, this type can pull content from external data sources, placeholders, or plugin integrations.

Usage[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/dynamic-pagination#usage "Direct link to Usage")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`items:  dynamic-list:    type: DYNAMIC_PAGINATION    slots:      - 10-16      - 19-25    source: "players"    item:      material: PLAYER_HEAD      player-head: "%entry_name%"      name: "&a%entry_name%"`

Configuration[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/dynamic-pagination#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Property | Description | Required |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `type` | Must be `DYNAMIC_PAGINATION` | Yes |
| `slots` | Slots where paginated items appear | Yes |
| `source` | Data source identifier | Yes |
| `item` | Item template for each entry | Yes |

Example[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/dynamic-pagination#example "Direct link to Example")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Player List[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/dynamic-pagination#player-list "Direct link to Player List")

`size: 54name: "&8Online Players"items:  player-list:    type: DYNAMIC_PAGINATION    slots:      - 10-16      - 19-25      - 28-34    source: "online_players"    item:      material: PLAYER_HEAD      player-head: "%entry_name%"      name: "&a&l%entry_name%"      lore:        - "&7Click to view profile"    actions:      - type: player-command        commands:          - "profile %entry_name%"  # Navigation  previous:    type: PREVIOUS    slot: 48    is-permanent: true    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&c&lPrevious"  next:    type: NEXT    slot: 50    is-permanent: true    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&a&lNext"  # Page info  info:    slot: 49    is-permanent: true    item:      material: PAPER      name: "&7Page %page%/%max_page%"`

Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/dynamic-pagination#placeholders "Direct link to Placeholders")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Placeholder | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `%entry_name%` | Entry name/identifier |
| `%entry_index%` | Entry index in the list |
| `%page%` | Current page number |
| `%max_page%` | Total number of pages |

Next Steps[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/dynamic-pagination#next-steps "Direct link to Next Steps")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Learn about [PAGINATION](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/pagination) for static pagination
*   See [INPUT](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/input) for player input handling

[](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/pagination)[](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/input)

*   [Usage](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/dynamic-pagination#usage)
*   [Configuration](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/dynamic-pagination#configuration)
*   [Example](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/dynamic-pagination#example)
    *   [Player List](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/dynamic-pagination#player-list)

*   [Placeholders](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/dynamic-pagination#placeholders)
*   [Next Steps](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/dynamic-pagination#next-steps)
