Page 23/41
URL: https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands
Source: https://r.jina.ai/http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands
================================================================================
Title: Custom Commands | GroupeZ Docs

URL Source: http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands

Markdown Content:
zMenu allows you to create custom commands that open your inventories. Instead of using `/zm open shop`, players can simply type `/shop`.

Configuration File[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#configuration-file "Direct link to Configuration File")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Custom commands are defined in `plugins/zMenu/commands/commands.yml`.

Basic Structure[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#basic-structure "Direct link to Basic Structure")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`commands:  shop:    command: shop    inventory: shop_menu`

This creates the `/shop` command that opens the `shop_menu` inventory.

Configuration Options[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#configuration-options "Direct link to Configuration Options")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Summary Table[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#summary-table "Direct link to Summary Table")

| Key | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `command` | String | Yes | Main command players will type |
| `inventory` | String | Yes | Name of the inventory to open |
| `permission` | String | No | Permission required to use the command |
| `deny-message` | String | No | Message shown when user lacks permission |
| `aliases` | List | No | Alternative command names |
| `arguments` | List | No | Command arguments with validation |
| `actions` | List | No | Actions executed when command runs |
| `console-can-use` | Boolean | No | Defaults to `false`. If `true`, allows the console to execute the command |

* * *

### command[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#command "Direct link to command")

**Required.** The command players will type.

`command: shop`

* * *

### inventory[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#inventory "Direct link to inventory")

**Required.** The inventory to open when the command is used. You can optionally prefix with the plugin name.

`inventory: "shop"  # Opens inventories/shop.yml# Or with plugin prefixinventory: "MyPlugin:shop"  # Opens shop inventory from MyPlugin`

* * *

### permission[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#permission "Direct link to permission")

Optional permission required to use the command.

`permission: "myserver.shop"`

* * *

### deny-message[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#deny-message "Direct link to deny-message")

Custom message displayed when a player doesn't have the required permission.

`deny-message: "&cYou don't have access to the shop!"`

* * *

### aliases[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#aliases "Direct link to aliases")

Alternative command names.

`aliases:  - store  - market  - buy`

This allows `/store`, `/market`, and `/buy` to work the same as `/shop`.

* * *

### actions[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#actions "Direct link to actions")

Actions to execute when the command is used (before opening the inventory).

`actions:  - type: message    messages:      - "&aOpening the shop..."  - type: sound    sound: BLOCK_CHEST_OPEN`

* * *

### arguments[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#arguments "Direct link to arguments")

Define command arguments with validation and auto-completion.

`arguments:  - name: "category"    isRequired: false    auto-completion:      - "weapons"      - "armor"      - "tools"`

#### Argument Options[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#argument-options "Direct link to Argument Options")

| Key | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `name` | String | **Required.** Identifier for the argument |
| `type` | String | Validator type for the argument (see below) |
| `isRequired` | Boolean | Whether the argument must be provided (default: `false`) |
| `performMainAction` | Boolean | Whether to execute main command actions when this argument is used (default: `true`) |
| `auto-completion` | List | Suggested values for tab-completion |
| `actions` | List | Actions to execute specific to this argument |

#### Argument Type Validators[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#argument-type-validators "Direct link to Argument Type Validators")

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `online-player` | Validates that the argument is an online player name |
| `player` | Validates that the argument is a player (online or offline) |
| `integer` | Validates that the argument is a whole number |
| `double` | Validates that the argument is a decimal number |
| `boolean` | Validates that the argument is true/false |
| `material` | Validates that the argument is a valid Minecraft material |
| `world` | Validates that the argument is a valid world name |
| `entity-type` | Validates that the argument is a valid entity type |
| `location` | Validates that the argument is a valid location |

#### Argument Example with Type Validation[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#argument-example-with-type-validation "Direct link to Argument Example with Type Validation")

`arguments:  - name: "player"    type: online-player    isRequired: true    auto-completion: "@players"  - name: "amount"    type: integer    isRequired: false    auto-completion:      - "1"      - "10"      - "64"`

Examples[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#examples "Direct link to Examples")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Simple Shop Command[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#simple-shop-command "Direct link to Simple Shop Command")

`commands:  shop:    command: shop    inventory: shop    permission: "server.shop"    deny-message: "&cYou need to be a member to access the shop!"    aliases:      - store      - market`

### Warps Command[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#warps-command "Direct link to Warps Command")

`commands:  warps:    command: warps    inventory: warps_menu    permission: "server.warps"    deny-message: "&cYou don't have permission to use warps!"    aliases:      - warp      - teleport    actions:      - type: message        messages:          - "&7Opening warps menu..."`

`commands:  adminmenu:    command: adminmenu    inventory: admin_panel    permission: "server.admin.menu"    aliases:      - admin      - apanel`

`commands:  menu:    command: menu    inventory: main_menu    aliases:      - gui      - m  help:    command: help    inventory: help_menu    permission: "server.help"  rules:    command: rules    inventory: rules_menu`

### Server Information[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#server-information "Direct link to Server Information")

`commands:  info:    command: /info    inventory: server_info    aliases:      - serverinfo      - about    actions:      - type: sound        sound: ENTITY_EXPERIENCE_ORB_PICKUP`

Multiple Command Files[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#multiple-command-files "Direct link to Multiple Command Files")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can organize commands in multiple files:

`plugins/zMenu/commands/├── commands.yml├── shop/│   └── shop_commands.yml├── admin/│   └── admin_commands.yml└── social/    └── social_commands.yml`

Each file follows the same format:

`# commands/shop/shop_commands.ymlcommands:  shop:    command: shop    inventory: shop_main  buyweapons:    command: /buyweapons    inventory: shop_weapons`

Command Arguments[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#command-arguments "Direct link to Command Arguments")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Basic Arguments[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#basic-arguments "Direct link to Basic Arguments")

`commands:  give-menu:    command: /givemenu    inventory: give_menu    permission: "server.admin"    arguments:      - name: "player"        type: online-player        isRequired: true        auto-completion: "@players"  # Auto-complete with online players`

### Multiple Arguments[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#multiple-arguments "Direct link to Multiple Arguments")

`commands:  category:    command: /category    inventory: category_menu    arguments:      - name: "type"        isRequired: true        auto-completion:          - "weapons"          - "armor"          - "tools"          - "food"      - name: "page"        type: integer        isRequired: false        auto-completion:          - "1"          - "2"          - "3"`

### Arguments with performMainAction[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#arguments-with-performmainaction "Direct link to Arguments with performMainAction")

Use `performMainAction: false` to create commands that process arguments without opening the main inventory.

`commands:  pay:    command: /pay    inventory: payment_confirm    arguments:      - name: "player"        type: online-player        isRequired: true        auto-completion: "@players"      - name: "amount"        type: integer        isRequired: true        performMainAction: true  # Opens inventory after validation        actions:          - type: message            messages:              - "&aPreparing payment of %args_1% to %args_0%..."`

### Arguments with Specific Actions[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#arguments-with-specific-actions "Direct link to Arguments with Specific Actions")

Each argument can have its own actions that execute when that argument is provided.

`commands:  teleport:    command: /tp    permission: "server.teleport"    arguments:      - name: "player"        type: online-player        isRequired: true        performMainAction: false  # Don't open inventory        actions:          - type: console_command            commands:              - "tp %player% %args_0%"          - type: message            messages:              - "&aTeleported to %args_0%!"`

Conflicting Commands[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#conflicting-commands "Direct link to Conflicting Commands")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If your command conflicts with another plugin:

1.   **Change the command name** to something unique
2.   **Use aliases** as the main entry point
3.   **Check plugin load order** in server configuration

tip

If a command like `/shop` is taken by another plugin, use a unique command like `/zmshop` and add `/shop` as an alias. zMenu will try to register the alias.

Permission Examples[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#permission-examples "Direct link to Permission Examples")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### With LuckPerms[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#with-luckperms "Direct link to With LuckPerms")

`# Give permission to use shop/lp group default permission set server.shop true# Admin menu for admins only/lp group admin permission set server.admin.menu true`

### Deny Message[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#deny-message-1 "Direct link to Deny Message")

Players without permission see the default "no permission" message. Customize this in your messages configuration.

Reloading Commands[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#reloading-commands "Direct link to Reloading Commands")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After modifying command files:

`/zm reload command           # Reload all commands/zm reload command shop      # Reload specific command`

Complete Example[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#complete-example "Direct link to Complete Example")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`# commands/commands.ymlcommands:  # Main server menu  menu:    command: menu    inventory: main_menu    aliases:      - gui      - server    actions:      - type: sound        sound: BLOCK_CHEST_OPEN  # Shop with permission  shop:    command: shop    inventory: shop_main    permission: "server.shop"    aliases:      - store      - market      - buy  # VIP shop  vipshop:    command: /vipshop    inventory: vip_shop    permission: "server.vip.shop"    aliases:      - vs  # Warps menu  warps:    command: warps    inventory: warps_menu    permission: "server.warps"    aliases:      - warp      - w  # Player profile  profile:    command: /profile    inventory: player_profile    aliases:      - stats      - me  # Help menu  help:    command: /serverhelp    inventory: help_menu    aliases:      - faq      - info  # Admin panel  admin:    command: /adminpanel    inventory: admin_menu    permission: "server.admin"    aliases:      - ap      - adminmenu`

Best Practices[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#best-practices "Direct link to Best Practices")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.   **Use intuitive names**: `/shop` not `/spm`
2.   **Add useful aliases**: Common variations and shortcuts
3.   **Set appropriate permissions**: Restrict sensitive menus
4.   **Keep it organized**: Use subfolders for large setups
5.   **Document commands**: Comment your YAML files
6.   **Test thoroughly**: Verify commands work as expected

Next Steps[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/custom-commands#next-steps "Direct link to Next Steps")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Configure the main [config.yml](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml)
*   Learn about [Player Data](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/player-data)
*   Set up [Global Placeholders](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders)

Title: Global Placeholders | GroupeZ Docs

URL Source: http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders

Markdown Content:
*   [](https://docs.groupez.dev/)
*   Configurations
*   Global Placeholders

Global Placeholders
-------------------

Global placeholders allow you to define values in one place and use them across all your inventories. This is useful for server information, URLs, and other values you might want to change centrally.

Configuration File[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#configuration-file "Direct link to Configuration File")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Global placeholders are defined in `plugins/zMenu/global-placeholders.yml`.

Basic Usage[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#basic-usage "Direct link to Basic Usage")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Defining Global Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#defining-global-placeholders "Direct link to Defining Global Placeholders")

`# global-placeholders.ymlserver-name: "My Awesome Server"server-ip: "play.myserver.com"discord: "discord.gg/myserver"website: "https://myserver.com"store: "https://store.myserver.com"version: "1.0.0"`

### Using Global Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#using-global-placeholders "Direct link to Using Global Placeholders")

Access them with `%zmenu_global_placeholders_<key>%`:

`# In your inventoryitems:  server-info:    slot: 4    item:      material: BOOK      name: "&6&l%zmenu_global_placeholders_server-name%"      lore:        - "&7IP: &f%zmenu_global_placeholders_server-ip%"        - "&7Discord: &9%zmenu_global_placeholders_discord%"        - "&7Website: &b%zmenu_global_placeholders_website%"`

Advanced Features[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#advanced-features "Direct link to Advanced Features")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### List Values[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#list-values "Direct link to List Values")

You can define lists of values:

`# global-placeholders.ymlrules:  - "&7- Be respectful to others"  - "&7- No cheating or hacking"  - "&7- No advertising"  - "&7- Have fun!"`

### Nested Values[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#nested-values "Direct link to Nested Values")

Use dots for organization (they become part of the key):

`# global-placeholders.ymlsocial.discord: "discord.gg/myserver"social.twitter: "@MyServer"social.youtube: "youtube.com/myserver"prices.vip: "9.99"prices.mvp: "19.99"prices.legend: "49.99"`

Usage:

`lore:  - "&7Discord: %zmenu_global_placeholders_social.discord%"  - "&7VIP Price: $%zmenu_global_placeholders_prices.vip%"`

Examples[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#examples "Direct link to Examples")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Server Information Menu[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#server-information-menu "Direct link to Server Information Menu")

`# global-placeholders.ymlserver-name: "CraftWorld"server-ip: "play.craftworld.net"discord: "discord.gg/craftworld"website: "https://craftworld.net"owner: "Notch"founded: "2020"`

`# inventories/server_info.ymlname: "&6Server Information"size: 27items:  info:    slot: 13    item:      material: BOOK      name: "&6&l%zmenu_global_placeholders_server-name%"      lore:        - "&8&m─────────────────"        - ""        - "&7IP: &f%zmenu_global_placeholders_server-ip%"        - "&7Discord: &9%zmenu_global_placeholders_discord%"        - "&7Website: &b%zmenu_global_placeholders_website%"        - ""        - "&7Owner: &e%zmenu_global_placeholders_owner%"        - "&7Founded: &a%zmenu_global_placeholders_founded%"        - ""        - "&8&m─────────────────"`

### Store Prices[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#store-prices "Direct link to Store Prices")

`# global-placeholders.ymlrank.vip.price: "9.99"rank.vip.name: "&a&lVIP"rank.mvp.price: "19.99"rank.mvp.name: "&b&lMVP"rank.legend.price: "49.99"rank.legend.name: "&6&lLEGEND"`

`# inventories/ranks.ymlitems:  vip:    slot: 11    item:      material: IRON_BLOCK      name: "%zmenu_global_placeholders_rank.vip.name%"      lore:        - "&7Price: &a$%zmenu_global_placeholders_rank.vip.price%"  mvp:    slot: 13    item:      material: GOLD_BLOCK      name: "%zmenu_global_placeholders_rank.mvp.name%"      lore:        - "&7Price: &a$%zmenu_global_placeholders_rank.mvp.price%"  legend:    slot: 15    item:      material: DIAMOND_BLOCK      name: "%zmenu_global_placeholders_rank.legend.name%"      lore:        - "&7Price: &a$%zmenu_global_placeholders_rank.legend.price%"`

### Centralized Colors/Themes[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#centralized-colorsthemes "Direct link to Centralized Colors/Themes")

`# global-placeholders.ymlcolor.primary: "&6"color.secondary: "&7"color.success: "&a"color.error: "&c"color.info: "&b"prefix.shop: "&6&lSHOP &8»"prefix.warp: "&5&lWARP &8»"prefix.admin: "&c&lADMIN &8»"`

`# Use in inventoriesitems:  item:    item:      name: "%zmenu_global_placeholders_color.primary%My Item"`

Benefits[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#benefits "Direct link to Benefits")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.   **Centralized Management**: Change values in one place
2.   **Consistency**: Ensure the same values across all menus
3.   **Easy Updates**: Update server IP, Discord link, etc. once
4.   **Organization**: Keep configuration values together
5.   **No Restarts**: Changes apply after `/zm reload`

Comparison with Local Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#comparison-with-local-placeholders "Direct link to Comparison with Local Placeholders")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Feature | Global Placeholders | Local Placeholders |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Scope | All inventories | Single inventory |
| File | `global-placeholders.yml` | Inside inventory file |
| Access | `%zmenu_global_placeholders_key%` | `%key%` |
| Use case | Server-wide values | Inventory-specific values |

### Local Placeholders Example[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#local-placeholders-example "Direct link to Local Placeholders Example")

`# In inventory filelocal-placeholders:  category: "Weapons"  discount: "20%"items:  header:    item:      name: "&6%category% Shop"      lore:        - "&7Sale: %discount% off!"`

Reloading[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#reloading "Direct link to Reloading")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After making changes to `global-placeholders.yml`:

`/zm reload config`

Or reload everything:

`/zm reload`

Best Practices[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#best-practices "Direct link to Best Practices")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.   **Use descriptive keys**: `server-ip` not `ip`
2.   **Group related values**: Use dot notation like `social.discord`
3.   **Document your placeholders**: Add comments in the YAML file
4.   **Keep it organized**: Group by purpose (social, prices, colors)
5.   **Don't overuse**: Only use for truly global values

Next Steps[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/global-placeholders#next-steps "Direct link to Next Steps")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Learn about [Patterns](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/patterns) for reusable templates
*   See [Player Data](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/player-data) for per-player values
*   Configure the [config.yml](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/config-yml) file

SWITCH Button Type
==================

The `SWITCH` button type displays different items based on a placeholder value. This allows you to create dynamic buttons that change appearance based on player data or other conditions.

Usage[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/switch#usage "Direct link to Usage")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`items:  toggle:    type: SWITCH    slot: 13    key: "%zmenu_player_value_notifications%"buttons:        "true":          item:            material: LIME_DYE            name: "&a&lNotifications: ON"          lore:            - "&7Click to disable"        actions:          - type: data            action: SET            key: "notifications"            value: "false"          - type: refresh      "false":        slot: 13        item:          material: GRAY_DYE          name: "&7&lNotifications: OFF"          lore:            - "&7Click to enable"        actions:          - type: data            action: SET            key: "notifications"            value: "true"          - type: refresh`

Properties[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/switch#properties "Direct link to Properties")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### placeholder[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/switch#placeholder "Direct link to placeholder")

**Required.** The placeholder to evaluate for determining which button to display.

`key: "%zmenu_player_value_setting%"`

* * *

### buttons[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/switch#buttons "Direct link to buttons")

**Required.** A map of values to button configurations. The key is the placeholder result, and the value is the button config to display.

`buttons:  "value1":    item:      material: DIAMOND    actions:      - type: message        messages: ["Value is 1"]  "value2":    item:      material: EMERALD    actions:      - type: message        messages: ["Value is 2"]`

* * *

### default[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/switch#default "Direct link to default")

Button to display when the placeholder value doesn't match any defined buttons.

`default:  item:    material: BARRIER    name: "&cUnknown State"`

Examples[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/switch#examples "Direct link to Examples")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Toggle Setting[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/switch#toggle-setting "Direct link to Toggle Setting")

`items:  toggle-pvp:    type: SWITCH    slot: 13    key: "%zmenu_player_value_pvp_enabled%"    buttons:      "true":        item:          material: DIAMOND_SWORD          name: "&c&lPvP: ENABLED"          lore:            - "&7You can be attacked by players"            - ""            - "&e▸ Click to disable"          glow: true        actions:          - type: data            action: SET            key: "pvp_enabled"            value: "false"          - type: message            messages:              - "&aPvP has been disabled!"          - type: sound            sound: BLOCK_NOTE_BLOCK_PLING          - type: refresh      "false":        slot: 13        item:          material: SHIELD          name: "&a&lPvP: DISABLED"          lore:            - "&7You are protected from players"            - ""            - "&e▸ Click to enable"        actions:          - type: data            action: SET            key: "pvp_enabled"            value: "true"          - type: message            messages:              - "&cPvP has been enabled!"          - type: sound            sound: ENTITY_ENDER_DRAGON_GROWL          - type: refresh    default:      item:        material: SHIELD        name: "&a&lPvP: DISABLED"      actions:        - type: data          action: SET          key: "pvp_enabled"          value: "true"        - type: refresh`

### Multi-State Button[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/switch#multi-state-button "Direct link to Multi-State Button")

`items:  difficulty:    type: SWITCH    slot: 22    key: "%zmenu_player_value_difficulty%"    buttons:      "easy":        slot: 13        item:          material: LIME_WOOL          name: "&a&lDifficulty: EASY"          lore:            - "&7Current: Easy mode"            - ""            - "&e▸ Click to change to Normal"        actions:          - type: data            action: SET            key: "difficulty"            value: "normal"          - type: refresh      "normal":        slot: 13        item:          material: YELLOW_WOOL          name: "&e&lDifficulty: NORMAL"          lore:            - "&7Current: Normal mode"            - ""            - "&e▸ Click to change to Hard"        actions:          - type: data            action: SET            key: "difficulty"            value: "hard"          - type: refresh      "hard":        slot: 13        item:          material: RED_WOOL          name: "&c&lDifficulty: HARD"          lore:            - "&7Current: Hard mode"            - ""            - "&e▸ Click to change to Easy"        actions:          - type: data            action: SET            key: "difficulty"            value: "easy"          - type: refresh    default:      item:        material: YELLOW_WOOL        name: "&e&lDifficulty: NORMAL"      actions:        - type: data          action: SET          key: "difficulty"          value: "hard"        - type: refresh`

### Rank-Based Display[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/switch#rank-based-display "Direct link to Rank-Based Display")

`items:  rank-display:    type: SWITCH    slot: 4    key: "%luckperms_primary_group_name%"    buttons:      "default":        slot: 13        item:          material: COAL          name: "&7&lMember"          lore:            - "&7Your current rank"      "vip":        slot: 13        item:          material: IRON_INGOT          name: "&a&lVIP"          lore:            - "&7Your current rank"          glow: true      "mvp":        slot: 13        item:          material: GOLD_INGOT          name: "&6&lMVP"          lore:            - "&7Your current rank"          glow: true      "admin":        slot: 13        item:          material: DIAMOND          name: "&b&lAdmin"          lore:            - "&7Your current rank"          glow: true    default:      item:        material: COAL        name: "&7&lMember"`

### Progress Indicator[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/switch#progress-indicator "Direct link to Progress Indicator")

`items:  quest-status:    type: SWITCH    slot: 31    key: "%zmenu_player_value_quest_stage%"    buttons:      "0":        slot: 13        item:          material: PAPER          name: "&7&lQuest: Not Started"          lore:            - "&7Begin your adventure!"            - ""            - "&e▸ Click to start"        actions:          - type: data            action: SET            key: "quest_stage"            value: "1"          - type: message            messages:              - "&aQuest started! Talk to the village elder."          - type: refresh      "1":        slot: 13        item:          material: WRITABLE_BOOK          name: "&e&lQuest: In Progress"          lore:            - "&7Talk to the village elder"            - ""            - "&7Progress: &e1/3"      "2":        slot: 13        item:          material: WRITABLE_BOOK          name: "&e&lQuest: In Progress"          lore:            - "&7Collect 10 wheat"            - ""            - "&7Progress: &e2/3"      "3":        slot: 13        item:          material: ENCHANTED_BOOK          name: "&a&lQuest: Complete!"          lore:            - "&7Return for your reward"            - ""            - "&e▸ Click to claim"          glow: true        actions:          - type: console-command            commands:              - "give %player% diamond 5"          - type: data            action: SET            key: "quest_stage"            value: "done"          - type: message            messages:              - "&aYou received 5 diamonds!"          - type: refresh      "done":        slot: 13        item:          material: BOOK          name: "&8&lQuest: Completed"          lore:            - "&7You've completed this quest"    default:      item:        material: PAPER        name: "&7&lQuest: Not Started"`

Important Notes[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/switch#important-notes "Direct link to Important Notes")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.   **Use `refresh` action** - Always include a refresh action when changing the state
2.   **Quote string values** - Values like `"true"` and `"false"` need quotes
3.   **Provide default** - Always define a default for unexpected values
4.   **Player data integration** - Works great with `%zmenu_player_value_*%` placeholders

Common Use Cases[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/switch#common-use-cases "Direct link to Common Use Cases")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Toggle settings (on/off)
*   Multi-option selectors
*   Progress indicators
*   Rank-based displays
*   State machines
*   Conditional rewards

Best Practices[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/switch#best-practices "Direct link to Best Practices")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.   **Always refresh** after state changes
2.   **Use descriptive keys** for player data
3.   **Provide visual feedback** (sounds, messages)
4.   **Include default state** for new players
5.   **Use clear visual distinction** between states

Related Features[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/switch#related-features "Direct link to Related Features")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [Player Data](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/player-data) - Store player-specific values
*   [Placeholders](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/placeholders) - Dynamic values
*   [Actions](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/actions) - Execute on click

Title: BACK Button | GroupeZ Docs

URL Source: http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back

Markdown Content:
*   [](https://docs.groupez.dev/)
*   Configurations
*   Buttons
*   Button Types
*   BACK Button

BACK Button Type
----------------

The `BACK` button type returns the player to the previously opened inventory. zMenu maintains a history of opened inventories, allowing seamless navigation.

Usage[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back#usage "Direct link to Usage")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`items:  back:    type: BACK    slot: 45    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&c&lBack"      lore:        - "&7Return to previous menu"`

How It Works[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back#how-it-works "Direct link to How It Works")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.   Player opens Menu A
2.   Player clicks to open Menu B (history: [Menu A])
3.   Player clicks to open Menu C (history: [Menu A, Menu B])
4.   Player clicks BACK button → Returns to Menu B
5.   Player clicks BACK button → Returns to Menu A

If there's no previous inventory in history, clicking a BACK button does nothing.

Properties[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back#properties "Direct link to Properties")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `BACK` button accepts all standard button properties:

| Property | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `slot` / `slots` | Position(s) in inventory |
| `item` | Visual appearance |
| `sound` | Sound on click |
| `is-permanent` | Show on all pages |
| `view-requirement` | Conditions to see |

Examples[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back#examples "Direct link to Examples")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Basic Back Button[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back#basic-back-button "Direct link to Basic Back Button")

`items:  back:    type: BACK    slot: 45    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&c&lBack"    sound: UI_BUTTON_CLICK`

### Styled Back Button[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back#styled-back-button "Direct link to Styled Back Button")

`items:  back:    type: BACK    slot: 45    item:      material: PLAYER_HEAD      url: "eyJ0ZXh0dXJlcyI6eyJTS0lOIjp7InVybCI6Imh0dHA6Ly90ZXh0dXJlcy5taW5lY3JhZnQubmV0L3RleHR1cmUvYmQ2OWUwNmU1ZGFkZmQ4NGU1ZjNkMWMyMTA2M2YyNTUzYjJmYTk0NWVlMWQ0ZDcxNTJmZGM1NDI1YmMxMmE5In19"      name: "&c&l← Back"      lore:        - "&7Return to the previous menu"    sound: UI_BUTTON_CLICK`

### Permanent Back Button[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back#permanent-back-button "Direct link to Permanent Back Button")

`items:  back:    type: BACK    slot: 45    is-permanent: true    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&c&lBack"`

This shows the back button on all pages of a paginated inventory.

### Navigation Bar with Back[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back#navigation-bar-with-back "Direct link to Navigation Bar with Back")

`items:  back:    type: BACK    slot: 45    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&c&lBack"    sound: UI_BUTTON_CLICK  home:    type: HOME    slot: 49    item:      material: NETHER_STAR      name: "&e&lMain Menu"    sound: UI_BUTTON_CLICK  close:    slot: 53    close-inventory: true    item:      material: BARRIER      name: "&c&lClose"    sound: UI_BUTTON_CLICK`

### Conditional Back Button[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back#conditional-back-button "Direct link to Conditional Back Button")

Only show back button if there's a previous inventory:

`items:  back:    type: BACK    slot: 45    view-requirement:      requirements:        - type: placeholder          placeholder: "%zmenu_player_previous_inventories%"          action: SUPERIOR          value: 0    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&c&lBack"    else:      item:        material: GRAY_STAINED_GLASS_PANE        name: "&8"`

Alternative: Using Actions[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back#alternative-using-actions "Direct link to Alternative: Using Actions")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can also use the `back` action with a regular button:

`items:  back:    slot: 45    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&c&lBack"    actions:      - type: back`

The `BACK` button type is shorthand for this.

Common Patterns[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back#common-patterns "Direct link to Common Patterns")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Bottom Navigation Bar[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back#bottom-navigation-bar "Direct link to Bottom Navigation Bar")

`items:  nav-border-left:    slots:      - 45      - 46      - 47    item:      material: BLACK_STAINED_GLASS_PANE      name: "&8"  back:    type: BACK    slot: 48    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&c&lBack"  info:    slot: 49    item:      material: BOOK      name: "&e&lPage %page%/%max-page%"  home:    type: HOME    slot: 50    item:      material: NETHER_STAR      name: "&6&lHome"  nav-border-right:    slots:      - 51      - 52      - 53    item:      material: BLACK_STAINED_GLASS_PANE      name: "&8"`

Best Practices[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back#best-practices "Direct link to Best Practices")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.   **Place consistently** - Put back buttons in the same position across all menus
2.   **Use clear icons** - Arrows or left-pointing heads work well
3.   **Add sounds** - Provide audio feedback when navigating
4.   **Consider HOME** - For deep menu hierarchies, add a HOME button too
5.   **Make permanent** - In paginated menus, use `is-permanent: true`

*   [HOME](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/home) - Return to the first inventory in history
*   [MAIN_MENU](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/mainmenu) - Open the configured main menu
*   [INVENTORY](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory) - Open a specific inventory

Next Steps[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back#next-steps "Direct link to Next Steps")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   View all [Button Types](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/none)

Title: INVENTORY Button | GroupeZ Docs

URL Source: http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory

Published Time: Thu, 05 Mar 2026 10:45:40 GMT

Markdown Content:
*   [](https://docs.groupez.dev/)
*   Configurations
*   Buttons
*   Button Types
*   INVENTORY Button

INVENTORY Button Type
---------------------

The `INVENTORY` button type opens another inventory when clicked.

Usage[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#usage "Direct link to Usage")
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`items:  open-shop:    type: INVENTORY    slot: 13    inventory: "shop"    item:      material: GOLD_INGOT      name: "&e&lShop"      lore:        - "&7Click to open the shop"`

Properties[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#properties "Direct link to Properties")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### inventory[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#inventory "Direct link to inventory")

**Required.** The name of the inventory to open.

`items:  open-menu:    type: INVENTORY    slot: 0    inventory: "my_other_menu"`

The inventory name corresponds to the file name (without `.yml`) in the `inventories/` folder.

* * *

### plugin[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#plugin "Direct link to plugin")

Specify which plugin's inventory to open (for cross-plugin support).

`items:  open-external:    type: INVENTORY    slot: 0    inventory: "external_menu"    plugin: "OtherPlugin"`

* * *

### arguments[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#arguments "Direct link to arguments")

Pass arguments to the target inventory.

`items:  open_with_args:    type: INVENTORY    slot: 0    inventory: "category_menu"    arguments:      - "swords"      - "%player%"`

* * *

### page[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#page "Direct link to page")

Open the inventory at a specific page.

`items:  open_page_3:    type: INVENTORY    slot: 0    inventory: "paginated_menu"    to-page: 3`

Examples[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#examples "Direct link to Examples")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Basic Menu Navigation[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#basic-menu-navigation "Direct link to Basic Menu Navigation")

`items:  shop:    type: INVENTORY    slot: 11    inventory: "shop"    item:      material: GOLD_INGOT      name: "&e&lShop"      lore:        - "&7Buy and sell items"        - ""        - "&e▸ Click to open"  warps:    type: INVENTORY    slot: 13    inventory: "warps"    item:      material: ENDER_PEARL      name: "&5&lWarps"      lore:        - "&7Teleport around the world"        - ""        - "&e▸ Click to open"  settings:    type: INVENTORY    slot: 15    inventory: "settings"    item:      material: COMPARATOR      name: "&c&lSettings"      lore:        - "&7Configure your preferences"        - ""        - "&e▸ Click to open"`

### Category Selection[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#category-selection "Direct link to Category Selection")

`# Main menuitems:  swords:    type: INVENTORY    slot: 10    inventory: "shop_swords"    item:      material: DIAMOND_SWORD      name: "&b&lSwords"  armor:    type: INVENTORY    slot: 12    inventory: "shop_armor"    item:      material: DIAMOND_CHESTPLATE      name: "&9&lArmor"  tools:    type: INVENTORY    slot: 14    inventory: "shop_tools"    item:      material: DIAMOND_PICKAXE      name: "&a&lTools"  food:    type: INVENTORY    slot: 16    inventory: "shop_food"    item:      material: GOLDEN_APPLE      name: "&6&lFood"`

### With Requirements[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#with-requirements "Direct link to With Requirements")

`items:  vip-shop:    type: INVENTORY    slot: 22    inventory: "vip_shop"    item:      material: DIAMOND_BLOCK      name: "&b&lVIP Shop"      lore:        - "&7Exclusive VIP items"    view-requirement:      requirements:        - type: permission          permission: "server.vip"    else:      item:        material: COAL_BLOCK        name: "&8&lVIP Shop"        lore:          - "&cRequires VIP rank"`

### Opening at Specific Page[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#opening-at-specific-page "Direct link to Opening at Specific Page")

`items:  page_1:    type: INVENTORY    slot: 10    inventory: "items_catalog"    page: 1    item:      material: PAPER      name: "&7Page 1"  page_2:    type: INVENTORY    slot: 11    inventory: "items_catalog"    page: 2    item:      material: PAPER      name: "&7Page 2"  page_3:    type: INVENTORY    slot: 12    inventory: "items_catalog"    to-page: 3    item:      material: PAPER      name: "&7Page 3"`

Alternative: Using Actions[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#alternative-using-actions "Direct link to Alternative: Using Actions")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can also open inventories using the `inventory` action with a `NONE` button:

`items:  open-shop:    slot: 13    item:      material: GOLD_INGOT      name: "&e&lShop"    actions:      - type: inventory        inventory: "shop"`

The `INVENTORY` button type is shorthand for this common pattern.

Navigation History[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#navigation-history "Direct link to Navigation History")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When using `INVENTORY` buttons, zMenu maintains a navigation history. This allows [BACK](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back) buttons to return to the previous menu.

The history is automatically managed - you don't need to configure anything special.

Best Practices[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#best-practices "Direct link to Best Practices")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.   **Use clear naming** for inventory files to easily identify them
2.   **Add visual feedback** with sounds when opening menus
3.   **Use requirements** to restrict access to certain menus
4.   **Provide locked states** with `else` for restricted menus
5.   **Organize in folders** for complex menu structures

Next Steps[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#next-steps "Direct link to Next Steps")
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Learn about [BACK](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back) buttons for navigation
*   Create [Multi-page Inventories](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/next) with pagination
*   See all [Button Properties](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/button)

[](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/none)[](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back)

*   [Usage](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#usage)
*   [Properties](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#properties)
    *   [inventory](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#inventory)
    *   [plugin](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#plugin)
    *   [arguments](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#arguments)
    *   [page](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory#page)

Title: NEXT Button | GroupeZ Docs

Markdown Content:
*   [](https://docs.groupez.dev/)
*   Configurations
*   Buttons
*   Button Types
*   NEXT Button

NEXT Button Type
----------------

The `NEXT` button type navigates to the next page in a paginated inventory.

Usage[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/next#usage "Direct link to Usage")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`items:  next:    type: NEXT    slot: 53    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&a&lNext Page →"      lore:        - "&7Go to page %zmenu_player_next_page%"`

How Pagination Works[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/next#how-pagination-works "Direct link to How Pagination Works")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Pagination is automatic when a button uses multiple slots and there's more content than available slots:

`items:  shop-items:    slots:      - 10-16      - 19-25      - 28-34    # This creates 21 slots per page    # If you have 42 items, it creates 2 pages`

The `NEXT` button only appears/works when there are more pages available.

Properties[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/next#properties "Direct link to Properties")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Property | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `slot` / `slots` | Position in inventory |
| `item` | Visual appearance |
| `sound` | Sound on click |
| `is-permanent` | Show on all pages (recommended) |

Examples[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/next#examples "Direct link to Examples")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Basic Next Button[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/next#basic-next-button "Direct link to Basic Next Button")

`items:  next:    type: NEXT    slot: 53    is-permanent: true    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&a&lNext →"    sound: UI_BUTTON_CLICK`

### Styled Next Button[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/next#styled-next-button "Direct link to Styled Next Button")

`items:  next:    type: NEXT    slot: 53    is-permanent: true    item:      material: PLAYER_HEAD      url: "eyJ0ZXh0dXJlcyI6eyJTS0lOIjp7InVybCI6Imh0dHA6Ly90ZXh0dXJlcy5taW5lY3JhZnQubmV0L3RleHR1cmUvMmE2ZDE1YTUyNzNlNjE0YjY0YTQ4ZjE2OTIxMzYyMmZjNGRkOTJlMWVhMTc4YzJiZDY1NzI3NDVhYWE2NTRiIn19"      name: "&a&lNext Page →"      lore:        - "&7Current: &f%page%"        - "&7Go to: &f%zmenu_player_next_page%"    sound: ITEM_BOOK_PAGE_TURN`

### Navigation Pair (Previous & Next)[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/next#navigation-pair-previous--next "Direct link to Navigation Pair (Previous & Next)")

`items:  previous:    type: PREVIOUS    slot: 45    is-permanent: true    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&c&l← Previous"    sound: UI_BUTTON_CLICK  page-info:    slot: 49    is-permanent: true    item:      material: PAPER      name: "&e&lPage %page%/%max-page%"      lore:        - "&7Navigate through pages"  next:    type: NEXT    slot: 53    is-permanent: true    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&a&lNext →"    sound: UI_BUTTON_CLICK`

### Hide When No More Pages[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/next#hide-when-no-more-pages "Direct link to Hide When No More Pages")

`items:  next:    type: NEXT    slot: 53    is-permanent: true    view-requirement:      requirements:        - type: placeholder          placeholder: "%zmenu_player_page%"          action: INFERIOR          value: "%zmenu_player_max_page%"    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&a&lNext →"    else:      item:        material: GRAY_STAINED_GLASS_PANE        name: "&8"`

Complete Paginated Inventory Example[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/next#complete-paginated-inventory-example "Direct link to Complete Paginated Inventory Example")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`name: "&6&lShop &8(&7Page %page%/%max-page%&8)"size: 54enable: truefillItem:  material: BLACK_STAINED_GLASS_PANE  name: "&8"items:  # Top border  top-border:    slots:      - 0-8    item:      material: BLUE_STAINED_GLASS_PANE      name: "&8"  # Shop items - these will paginate  shop-items:    slots:      - 10-16      - 19-25      - 28-34    # Define multiple items that fill these slots    # If there are more items than slots, pages are created  # Bottom border  bottom-border:    slots:      - 36-44    is-permanent: true    item:      material: BLUE_STAINED_GLASS_PANE      name: "&8"  # Navigation  previous:    type: PREVIOUS    slot: 45    is-permanent: true    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&c&l← Previous"    sound: UI_BUTTON_CLICK  back:    type: BACK    slot: 48    is-permanent: true    item:      material: DARK_OAK_DOOR      name: "&7&lBack to Menu"    sound: UI_BUTTON_CLICK  page-info:    slot: 49    is-permanent: true    item:      material: BOOK      name: "&e&lPage %page%/%max-page%"  close:    slot: 50    is-permanent: true    close-inventory: true    item:      material: BARRIER      name: "&c&lClose"    sound: UI_BUTTON_CLICK  next:    type: NEXT    slot: 53    is-permanent: true    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&a&lNext →"    sound: UI_BUTTON_CLICK`

Placeholders for Pagination[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/next#placeholders-for-pagination "Direct link to Placeholders for Pagination")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Placeholder | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `%page%` | Current page number |
| `%maxPage%` | Total number of pages |
| `%max-page%` | Same as maxPage |
| `%zmenu_player_page%` | Current page (PAPI) |
| `%zmenu_player_max_page%` | Max pages (PAPI) |
| `%zmenu_player_next_page%` | Next page number |
| `%zmenu_player_previous_page%` | Previous page number |

Best Practices[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/next#best-practices "Direct link to Best Practices")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.   **Use `is-permanent: true`** so navigation appears on all pages
2.   **Add page info** between Previous/Next buttons
3.   **Use sounds** for feedback when changing pages
4.   **Consider hiding** buttons when at first/last page
5.   **Place consistently** at bottom row (slots 45 and 53)

*   [PREVIOUS](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/previous) - Navigate to previous page

*   [BACK](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back) - Return to previous inventory

Title: API Introduction | GroupeZ Docs

URL Source: http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/development/api-introduction

Published Time: Thu, 05 Mar 2026 10:45:39 GMT

Markdown Content:
*   [](https://docs.groupez.dev/)
*   Development
*   API Introduction

API Introduction
----------------

zMenu provides a comprehensive API for developers to integrate with and extend the plugin's functionality. This guide will help you get started with the zMenu API.

Javadoc[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/development/api-introduction#javadoc "Direct link to Javadoc")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The complete API documentation is available at: [https://repo.groupez.dev/javadoc/releases/fr/maxlego08/menu/zmenu-api/1.1.0.6](https://repo.groupez.dev/javadoc/releases/fr/maxlego08/menu/zmenu-api/1.1.0.6)

Maven Repository[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/development/api-introduction#maven-repository "Direct link to Maven Repository")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add the GroupeZ repository to your `pom.xml`:

`<repositories>    <repository>        <id>groupez</id>        <url>https://repo.groupez.dev/releases</url>    </repository></repositories>`

Maven Dependency[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/development/api-introduction#maven-dependency "Direct link to Maven Dependency")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add the zMenu API as a dependency:

`<dependencies>    <dependency>        <groupId>fr.maxlego08.menu</groupId>        <artifactId>zmenu-api</artifactId>        <version>1.1.0.0</version>        <scope>provided</scope>    </dependency></dependencies>`

Gradle[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/development/api-introduction#gradle "Direct link to Gradle")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For Gradle users:

`repositories {    maven { url 'https://repo.groupez.dev/releases' }}dependencies {    compileOnly 'fr.maxlego08.menu:zmenu-api:1.1.0.0'}`

### Kotlin DSL[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/development/api-introduction#kotlin-dsl "Direct link to Kotlin DSL")

`repositories {    maven("https://repo.groupez.dev/releases")}dependencies {    compileOnly("fr.maxlego08.menu:zmenu-api:1.1.0.0")}`

Plugin Dependency[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/development/api-introduction#plugin-dependency "Direct link to Plugin Dependency")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add zMenu as a dependency in your `plugin.yml`:

`# Hard dependency (plugin won't load without zMenu)depend: [zMenu]# Soft dependency (plugin will load even without zMenu)softdepend: [zMenu]`

Getting the API[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/development/api-introduction#getting-the-api "Direct link to Getting the API")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Access the Plugin Instance[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/development/api-introduction#access-the-plugin-instance "Direct link to Access the Plugin Instance")

`import fr.maxlego08.menu.api.MenuPlugin;import org.bukkit.Bukkit;import org.bukkit.plugin.java.JavaPlugin;public class MyPlugin extends JavaPlugin {    private MenuPlugin menuPlugin;    @Override    public void onEnable() {        // Get zMenu instance        this.menuPlugin = (MenuPlugin) Bukkit.getPluginManager().getPlugin("zMenu");        if (this.menuPlugin == null) {            getLogger().severe("zMenu not found! Disabling plugin...");            Bukkit.getPluginManager().disablePlugin(this);            return;        }        getLogger().info("Successfully hooked into zMenu!");    }    public MenuPlugin getMenuPlugin() {        return this.menuPlugin;    }}`

### Safe Hook with Soft Dependency[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/development/api-introduction#safe-hook-with-soft-dependency "Direct link to Safe Hook with Soft Dependency")

`import fr.maxlego08.menu.api.MenuPlugin;import org.bukkit.Bukkit;import org.bukkit.plugin.Plugin;import org.bukkit.plugin.java.JavaPlugin;public class MyPlugin extends JavaPlugin {    private MenuPlugin menuPlugin;    private boolean zMenuEnabled = false;    @Override    public void onEnable() {        // Try to hook into zMenu        hookZMenu();        if (zMenuEnabled) {            getLogger().info("zMenu integration enabled!");            // Register zMenu-specific features        } else {            getLogger().info("zMenu not found, running without integration.");        }    }    private void hookZMenu() {        Plugin plugin = Bukkit.getPluginManager().getPlugin("zMenu");        if (plugin != null && plugin.isEnabled()) {            this.menuPlugin = (MenuPlugin) plugin;            this.zMenuEnabled = true;        }    }    public boolean isZMenuEnabled() {        return this.zMenuEnabled;    }    public MenuPlugin getMenuPlugin() {        return this.menuPlugin;    }}`

Core Interfaces[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/development/api-introduction#core-interfaces "Direct link to Core Interfaces")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The zMenu API provides several core interfaces:

### MenuPlugin[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/development/api-introduction#menuplugin "Direct link to MenuPlugin")

The main plugin interface providing access to all managers:

`MenuPlugin menuPlugin = ...;// Inventory managementInventoryManager inventoryManager = menuPlugin.getInventoryManager();// Button type registrationButtonManager buttonManager = menuPlugin.getButtonManager();// Command managementCommandManager commandManager = menuPlugin.getCommandManager();// Player data managementDataManager dataManager = menuPlugin.getDataManager();`

### Key Managers[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/development/api-introduction#key-managers "Direct link to Key Managers")

| Manager | Purpose |
| --- | --- |
| `InventoryManager` | Load, manage, and open inventories |
| `ButtonManager` | Register custom button types |
| `CommandManager` | Register custom commands |
| `DataManager` | Access player data storage |

API Structure[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/development/api-introduction#api-structure "Direct link to API Structure")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`fr.maxlego08.menu.api├── MenuPlugin              # Main plugin interface├── InventoryManager        # Inventory operations├── ButtonManager           # Button registration├── CommandManager          # Command handling├── DataManager             # Player data access├── button/│   ├── Button              # Button interface│   └── ButtonLoader        # Button loading├── action/│   ├── Action              # Action interface│   └── ActionLoader        # Action loading├── requirement/│   ├── Requirement         # Requirement interface│   └── Permissible         # Permission checking└── event/    ├── ButtonLoadEvent    ├── InventoryLoadEvent    └── PlayerOpenInventoryEvent`

Best Practices[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/development/api-introduction#best-practices "Direct link to Best Practices")
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.   **Always check for null** when getting the zMenu plugin instance
2.   **Use soft dependencies** if your plugin can function without zMenu
3.   **Don't store manager references** - get them fresh when needed
4.   **Handle exceptions** gracefully when working with inventories
5.   **Test thoroughly** with different zMenu versions

Complete Example Plugin[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/development/api-introduction#complete-example-plugin "Direct link to Complete Example Plugin")
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`package com.example.myplugin;import fr.maxlego08.menu.api.MenuPlugin;import fr.maxlego08.menu.api.InventoryManager;import org.bukkit.Bukkit;import org.bukkit.command.Command;import org.bukkit.command.CommandSender;import org.bukkit.entity.Player;import org.bukkit.plugin.java.JavaPlugin;public class MyPlugin extends JavaPlugin {    private MenuPlugin menuPlugin;    @Override    public void onEnable() {        // Hook into zMenu        this.menuPlugin = (MenuPlugin) Bukkit.getPluginManager().getPlugin("zMenu");        if (this.menuPlugin == null) {            getLogger().severe("zMenu is required!");            Bukkit.getPluginManager().disablePlugin(this);            return;        }        getLogger().info("MyPlugin enabled with zMenu integration!");    }    @Override    public boolean onCommand(CommandSender sender, Command command,                            String label, String[] args) {        if (!(sender instanceof Player)) {            sender.sendMessage("Players only!");            return true;        }        Player player = (Player) sender;        InventoryManager manager = menuPlugin.getInventoryManager();        // Open a zMenu inventory        manager.getInventory("my-menu").ifPresent(inv -> {            manager.openInventory(player, inv);        });        return true;    }}`

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PAGINATION Button Type
----------------------

This button type requires [zMenu+](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/zmenu-plus) to work.

The `PAGINATION` button type allows you to display paginated content in your menus. It automatically handles pagination of items across multiple pages.

Usage[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/pagination#usage "Direct link to Usage")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`items:  paginated-items:    type: PAGINATION    slots:      - 10-16      - 19-25      - 28-34    item:      material: STONE      name: "&7Item %index%"`

Configuration[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/pagination#configuration "Direct link to Configuration")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Property | Description | Required |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `type` | Must be `PAGINATION` | Yes |
| `slots` | Slots where paginated items appear | Yes |
| `item` | Item template for each entry | Yes |

Example[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/pagination#example "Direct link to Example")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Basic Pagination[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/pagination#basic-pagination "Direct link to Basic Pagination")

`size: 54name: "&8Paginated Menu"items:  # Paginated content area  content:    type: PAGINATION    slots:      - 10-16      - 19-25      - 28-34    item:      material: PAPER      name: "&e&lItem #%index%"      lore:        - "&7This is item number %index%"  # Navigation buttons  previous:    type: PREVIOUS    slot: 48    is-permanent: true    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&c&lPrevious Page"  next:    type: NEXT    slot: 50    is-permanent: true    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&a&lNext Page"`

Placeholders[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/pagination#placeholders "Direct link to Placeholders")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Placeholder | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `%index%` | Current item index |
| `%page%` | Current page number |
| `%max_page%` | Total number of pages |

Next Steps[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/pagination#next-steps "Direct link to Next Steps")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   See [NEXT](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/next) and [PREVIOUS](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/previous) for navigation buttons

Title: HOME Button | GroupeZ Docs

URL Source: http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/home

Markdown Content:

*   Configurations

*   HOME Button

HOME Button Type
----------------

The `HOME` button type returns the player to the very first inventory they opened in their navigation history. This is useful for deep menu hierarchies where players want to return to the start.

Usage[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/home#usage "Direct link to Usage")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`items:  home:    type: HOME    slot: 49    item:      material: NETHER_STAR      name: "&e&lHome"      lore:        - "&7Return to the main menu"`

How It Works[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/home#how-it-works "Direct link to How It Works")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Unlike the [BACK](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back) button which goes one step back, `HOME` clears the entire history and returns to the first inventory:

1.   Player opens Menu A (root)
2.   Player navigates: A → B → C → D
3.   Player clicks HOME → Returns directly to Menu A
4.   History is cleared

Difference from BACK and MAIN_MENU[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/home#difference-from-back-and-main_menu "Direct link to Difference from BACK and MAIN_MENU")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Button | Behavior |
| --- | --- |
| `BACK` | Goes to the previous inventory (one step) |
| `HOME` | Goes to the first inventory in history |
| `MAIN_MENU` | Opens the configured main menu (may be different) |

Examples[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/home#examples "Direct link to Examples")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Basic Home Button[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/home#basic-home-button "Direct link to Basic Home Button")

`items:  home:    type: HOME    slot: 49    item:      material: NETHER_STAR      name: "&e&lHome"    sound: ENTITY_ENDERMAN_TELEPORT`

### Styled Home Button[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/home#styled-home-button "Direct link to Styled Home Button")

`items:  home:    type: HOME    slot: 49    item:      material: PLAYER_HEAD      url: "eyJ0ZXh0dXJlcyI6eyJTS0lOIjp7InVybCI6Imh0dHA6Ly90ZXh0dXJlcy5taW5lY3JhZnQubmV0L3RleHR1cmUvYzVhMzFjNjQ1MzNlNTRhZmFjZjA0YzNhMTY3YzM4YjBhYjIzMjI3NjdmYjE2MWVmMTU5MjI5YTI4ZmJiN2EifX0="      name: "&6&l⌂ Home"      lore:        - "&7Return to the main menu"        - ""        - "&e▸ Click to go home"    sound: BLOCK_NOTE_BLOCK_CHIME`

### Navigation Bar with Home[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/home#navigation-bar-with-home "Direct link to Navigation Bar with Home")

`items:  back:    type: BACK    slot: 45    is-permanent: true    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&c&l← Back"    sound: UI_BUTTON_CLICK  previous:    type: PREVIOUS    slot: 47    is-permanent: true    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&7Previous"  home:    type: HOME    slot: 49    is-permanent: true    item:      material: NETHER_STAR      name: "&e&lHome"    sound: UI_BUTTON_CLICK  next:    type: NEXT    slot: 51    is-permanent: true    item:      material: ARROW      name: "&7Next"  close:    slot: 53    is-permanent: true    close-inventory: true    item:      material: BARRIER      name: "&c&lClose"`

### Conditional Home Button[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/home#conditional-home-button "Direct link to Conditional Home Button")

Only show when not at the root menu:

`items:  home:    type: HOME    slot: 49    view-requirement:      requirements:        - type: placeholder          placeholder: "%zmenu_player_previous_inventories%"          action: SUPERIOR          value: 0    item:      material: NETHER_STAR      name: "&e&lHome"    else:      item:        material: GRAY_STAINED_GLASS_PANE        name: "&8"`

When to Use[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/home#when-to-use "Direct link to When to Use")
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use `HOME` buttons when:

*   You have deep menu hierarchies (3+ levels)
*   Users need a quick way to restart navigation
*   Your menus branch into multiple categories

Best Practices[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/home#best-practices "Direct link to Best Practices")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.   **Place centrally** - Middle of the navigation bar (slot 49)
2.   **Use distinctive icon** - Nether star or house-shaped head
3.   **Add to all sub-menus** - Include in every non-root menu
4.   **Combine with BACK** - Give users both options
5.   **Use `is-permanent: true`** - Always visible on paginated menus

*   [BACK](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/back) - Go back one step
*   [MAIN_MENU](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/mainmenu) - Open configured main menu
*   [INVENTORY](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/inventory) - Open specific inventory

Next Steps[​](http://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/home#next-steps "Direct link to Next Steps")
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Learn about [MAIN_MENU](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/mainmenu) buttons
*   See the [JUMP](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/jump) button for page navigation
*   View all [Button Types](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/none)

[](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/previous)[](https://docs.groupez.dev/zmenu/configurations/buttons/types/jump)
